 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : The RCN Editor Staff                                          บ
 บ    Subject : Introduction : RCN Goes Biweekly                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Welcome to Reality Check Network, your #1 Warez E-mag!  And so we'd   บ
 บ  like to stay!  To meet further reader demand, the staff has decided that  บ
 บ  RCN will now be released on a biweekly schedule.  There won't be any      บ
 บ  less material found in each issue, the material will just be of even      บ
 บ  higher quality!  RCN will be released every other Sunday.  We believe     บ
 บ  that by giving ourselves more time between the release of each issue, we  บ
 บ  will be able to release a better RCN, and at the same time, the extra     บ
 บ  time will help create a more positive and less hectic work environment    บ
 บ  for the RCN Staff.                                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Again, you can always find Reality Check Network available on the     บ
 บ  WWW at HTTP://WWW.RCN.ORG/INDEX.HTML, as well as find some of our         บ
 บ  previous competition (though, unfortunately, none exists at the moment)   บ
 บ  and perhaps compare and contrast.  And as a final note, a little word     บ
 บ  about etiquette, purposefully placed at the END of the introduction.  I   บ
 บ  don't mind if you don't want to read an entire article or interview, and  บ
 บ  decide you've had enough in the middle, but if you're going to contact    บ
 บ  us with a complaint, make sure you HAVE read the entire text before       บ
 บ  doing so.  It doesn't look too impressive when you complain about         บ
 บ  something and our response to your complaint was in the body of the text  บ
 บ  all the while, but you were too lazy to find it.                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      As always, thanks for reading RCN, and don't hesitate to contact us!  บ
 บ  You can either join channel #RCN on the EFNet IRC network, or email us    บ
 บ  at an385786@anon.penet.fi.                                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ฿   ฿ฐ ฐ  ฐ ฐ ฐฐ ฐฐ฿฿ ฐฐฐฐ ฐ ฐฐฐ
฿฿฿฿฿฿     ฿   ฐ฿       ฐ   ฿฿฿
 ฿       ฿   ฐ  ฿   ฿฿฿฿      ฿      ฿ฐ฿
    ฿฿฿฿฿  ฿฿฿   ฿             ฿฿฿ฐ฿ฐ     ฿
                ฿฿฿฿        ฿  e d i t o r i a l !  ฿

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Dear RCN,                                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      As a former member of FBI, I would like to respond not only to the    บ
 บ  text file sent out by JDa, but also your dislike of Reflux and FBI.       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      For a short period during '95, I was an in-house courier for FBI.  I  บ
 บ  would distribute stuff, mostly though site couriering, when one day I     บ
 บ  noticed them releasing Bermuda Syndrome.  I had heard it was a really     บ
 บ  good game, even though it was big, so I tried it, and I definitely don't  บ
 บ  remember it being in Russian as Reflux claims.  FBI was a group           บ
 บ  dedicated to putting out good releases, not untranslated or non-working   บ
 บ  ones.  That was a great program, and I got much joy from letting others   บ
 บ  try it out, to see if they want to buy it, since I still feel that's the  บ
 บ  only right thing to do.  Remember, if everyone got the stuff for free,    บ
 บ  there wouldn't be any more of it!                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Even though I had long since left the group, I was appauled to find   บ
 บ  out that Reflux duped the release, but to make it worse, they were        บ
 บ  releasing it over half a year later!  Talk about sloppy.                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      In rebuttal to Reflux's claim that it was more than 50 disks so it    บ
 บ  shouldn't count as a real release, your release is too!  Bermuda          บ
 บ  Syndrome isn't much fun to play without all the addons, and if you add    บ
 บ  those onto the 50 disk total of Bermuda Syndrome, it's way over 60        บ
 บ  disks.                                                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Reflux claims that it's a new version.  If so, WHY NOT RELEASE A      บ
 บ  FUCKIN PATCH??  Because they're sloppy and led by that pussy Tklp (which  บ
 บ  stands for Tiny-Kocked-Little-Prick).                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I used to have respect for Tklp and his group, despite their major    บ
 บ  screw up with Quake, but after their duping and then DENYING the          บ
 บ  previous release's credibility, I have lost all faith in them.  I now     บ
 บ  agree with all of Rebel Chicken's criticism of ROR and Reflux, it is all  บ
 บ  viable.  This last mistake should prove it.                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      As for most people's treatment of FBI, I may no longer be a member,   บ
 บ  but I still have respect for them.  They weren't a tiny little group      บ
 บ  that barely got to the US, they were great.  I have now moved on to       บ
 บ  bigger and better things, as I am now a happy member of PTA, and active   บ
 บ  as ever.  But I have not forgotten my roots as so many people have.       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                               Signed,                      บ
 บ                                                  Ermac                     บ

 บ  Dear Razor,                                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      All I've heard this week from everyone I've talked to is either I     บ
 บ  can't connect to the sites, or "Why do I have ratios?"  So let's clear a  บ
 บ  few things up from the get go.  We send you all the info, if it is        บ
 บ  incorrect or you have trouble, simply email myself or Pitbull and we'll   บ
 บ  take care of it.  It's as simple as that.  ISPs unfortunatly change       บ
 บ  their IPs and subsequently your IPs occasionally.  Make sure you have     บ
 บ  supplied us your correct IP.  Try using NS Lookup to verify your IP.      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Now, as to ratios on the sites.  Unless you are a senior member, you  บ
 บ  have ratios.  Period, end of sentence.  Our sites are not huge            บ
 บ  stockpiles for everyone to plunder to be able to fill all the boards you  บ
 บ  call.  Sites operate the same way boards do.  They have ratios, time      บ
 บ  limits, and all the other goodies.  We have done our best to make sure    บ
 บ  sites have top 10 list and other ammenities to make them more appealing   บ
 บ  to our ppl to upload.  But no matter what we do, people just want to      บ
 บ  leech and leech and never upload.                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Now, the senior members are busy with the group, the day to day       บ
 บ  workings that few realize or understand.  It really makes me sick that    บ
 บ  there are few traders anymore.  It's time to go back to old school and    บ
 บ  learn how to trade.  If your aspirations are to be a courier all your     บ
 บ  life, then join fATE.  Razor is the best and I expect the best.  Traders  บ
 บ  trade files.  They do not leech from a site and then upload all those     บ
 บ  leeched files to a board.  The one way flow hardly benefits the group.    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I know on some sites, as with boards, it's hard to find files to      บ
 บ  upload.  Well guess what?  Life's hard, deal with it.  If you need help   บ
 บ  to learn how to become a trader, talk to some of the old school traders,  บ
 บ  like Third Son, Pharaoh, Mr. Skill, etc etc.  Now from time to time, we   บ
 บ  make exceptions and rewards for certain users, but don't expect that all  บ
 บ  the time.  It's time to grow up and face the real world.  And for anyone  บ
 บ  else that wants to whine know this, I have ratios on all the sites and    บ
 บ  you know how often I have free time to send files around.                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                               Signed,                      บ
 บ                                                  DruidKin                  บ
 บ                                                  Razor Coordinator         บ

 บ  Dear Anonymous,                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      You're going to be shocked when you read this reply.  Don't take it   บ
 บ  personally, it is not directed at you.  It's just a small bit about       บ
 บ  women that complain about their position in society and female rights.    บ
 บ  Rebel Chicken and I thought of this when we were at Safeway one day.      บ
 บ  I've been wanting to publish it for a while now, and it has absolutely    บ
 บ  nothing to do with warez, but it's something I've got to say and get      บ
 บ  e-mail back about, so people, don't hold back, I want to start a riot     บ
 บ  here, write me and tell me what you think of my little schpiel here.      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Once upon a time Rebel Chicken and I walked into a Safeway (it's a    บ
 บ  supermarket in the USA) to get something to eat while on an RCN break.    บ
 บ  We walked past the magazines, they were on the way to the cashier, when   บ
 บ  Rebel Chicken stopped and exclaimed "HUBBA HUBBA!!!"  I turned around     บ
 บ  and saw him checking out this babe on the front of some magazine.         บ
 บ  "Ehhhhhhh ---- heeeeeeeeeellllo!!"  I shouted back.  So we were checking  บ
 บ  out the women on the front of magazines and then Rebel Chicken noticed    บ
 บ  something (just when you thought he was actually looking at the women).   บ
 บ  He asked me "Did you notice how every magazine cover with a woman         บ
 บ  pictured on it has something about sex?"  Surely enough, he was right.    บ
 บ  We looked through about 25 magazines, and found only two that didn't.     บ
 บ  One issue of "Seventeen" and the other I don't remember.  Sorry guys, we  บ
 บ  didn't look at computer magazines.                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      So this is the conclusion I draw from all this.  Women have no right  บ
 บ  in hell to complain about being treated like sex toys.  I'll tell you     บ
 บ  right now, I definitely would NOT have minded treating those women as     บ
 บ  sex toys heheheh but there's no way they can try to tell me that they're  บ
 บ  just showing off beauty with no sexual connotation implied.  Before       บ
 บ  women can complain about being treated like objects and having a lower    บ
 บ  place in society, they need to think twice about their actions.  I don't  บ
 บ  mind the fact that beautiful women pose for magazines, but when every     บ
 บ  magazine with them says something like "20 tips to make your sex life     บ
 บ  better," "A quiz to see if you really know your way around your bed,"     บ
 บ  "5 women reveal the SEXXXIEST summer lingerie," "The moves the men        บ
 บ  really like," or "Sex tips for the new year, happy 1996!" it degrades     บ
 บ  the women's level in society.                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Right about now all the women's rights groups are telling me "I see   บ
 บ  nothing wrong with women doing this.  It shows that they feel more        บ
 บ  comfortable with issues about sex."  But so what?  Maybe the men don't.   บ
 บ  I don't know, I've never sexually molested a woman, and don't             บ
 บ  particularly plan on it, but others have, and I don't doubt that          บ
 บ  magazine covers such as the ones I'm speaking of had some part in it.     บ
 บ  So food for thought, and note that I'm not justifying Mike Tyson here,    บ
 บ  he's got the smallest knowledge : size of brain ratio I've ever seen.     บ
 บ  Would he really have patted that babe on her butt if she weren't wearing  บ
 บ  something so revealing?  When you invite people to a party, you can't     บ
 บ  expect to kick them out when they show up at your door, and when you      บ
 บ  invite trouble, you can't expect to kick its hand off your ass.           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      AAAAAND right about now the whole scene thinks I'm insane.  Oh well.  บ

 บ  someone want a personal heatlth manger or something that is very boring.  บ
 บ  3D Creative caladers and other lame releases I have seen passed around    บ
 บ  and when checking my BBS stats it seems that these files are never        บ
 บ  downloaded while Duke Nukem 3D on my board was downloaded 75 times!!!     บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ  quality things that a majority of people would like instead of wasting    บ
 บ  time cracking and passing around total junk.  For instance, I must have   บ
 บ  traded and seen over 5-7 gigs of files and how many of those files did I  บ
 บ  actually use?  Hardly any to be perfectly honest, in my time in the       บ
 บ  scene I might have used about 500 megs of all the things releases and a   บ
 บ  lot of the things that I used were the older files which I had to         บ
 บ  request because most of the newer things out there aren`t even that       บ
 บ  great to begin with.                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ  days are not making quality programs to crack but I do think they should  บ
 บ  have some pride and don't release "How to Type Faster Part 5" when they   บ
 บ  know people won't use it.                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ  something to do and they will trade almost everything and not even use    บ
 บ  it so release groups can get away with releasing junk because they know   บ
 บ  people will trade it no matter what it is.  So release groups that read   บ
 บ  this letter and think about the quality of your releases lately and ohh   บ

 บ  Dear RCN,                                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Hey guys, just wanted to respond to some of the editorials from RCN   บ
 บ  22.  To address the DCC courier's plea for DCC subdivisions in RiSC and   บ
 บ  Everlast, I must say it ain't gunna happen.  Although I'm in neither of   บ
 บ  these groups I can tell you, DCC Couriering isn't regarded as a           บ
 บ  prestigious way of moving files around.  Let me explain...    The elites  บ
 บ  of the scene pride themselves on doing something better than someone      บ
 บ  esle.  Which in fact is the definition of Elite.  Now with DCC            บ
 บ  couriering it is difficult, if at all possible to know who offered the    บ
 บ  release first.  How ever with boards and sites, only the fastest of the   บ
 บ  fast will upload a release.  In this respect DCC couriering is a          บ
 บ  non-competitive way of couriering, which is not regarded as much to the   บ
 บ  elites of the scene.                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      To respond to the disk size limit on games/utils.  Let me say there   บ
 บ  is nothing in the world more fun to a net monkey like me, then racing a   บ
 บ  50-60 disker all around the sites and causing a bit of havok to the       บ
 บ  people trying to upload.  Groups will continue to release big 50 disk     บ
 บ  crap to satisfy the couriers util someone decides to bring back the nuke  บ
 บ  x10.  My suggestion for the few people that do have nuke access, if it's  บ
 บ  lame nuke it, if it's hella old and people are still uploading it nuke    บ
 บ  it x1000 or so.  Better yet nuke that trader's account.                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      The reason dupes and fakes get spread so widely is that in ftp        บ
 บ  trading any hestitation even if only for a split second can cost you the  บ
 บ  weektop.  The people that should be the most prosecuted/nuked should be   บ
 บ  the people that bring these fakes/dupes to the net.                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Also I'd also like to mention that I'm seeing a trend here, where     บ
 บ  some couriers rely exclusively on pre-releases for all their upload       บ
 บ  credits.  However easy and/or effective this maybe, it is not the true    บ
 บ  showing of skill, and in my opinion people that should not be recognized  บ
 บ  as being couriers, but rather distributors for the release group they     บ
 บ  are in.                                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ  that's ok.  Information is power, arrogance and ignorance go hand in      บ

 บ  to the scene.  I had no power over what would happen to it.  I couldn't   บ
 บ  "not publish" it.  And do you know WHY he published it to the scene       บ
 บ  independently and didn't submit it to RCN?  Because he has no balls and   บ
 บ  didn't want to see the answer.  Too bad he saw it anyway.                 บ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Dear RCN,                                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Wassup Everyone!  This is just a little something I'd like to say     บ
 บ  about the interview done on AOD (Angel of Death) about LGN (Legion) and   บ
 บ  how they kicked out AcidPlain.                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Everything that AOD had said was true.  I was in the group for about  บ
 บ  two days.  If many of you don't remember, I was the one who constructed   บ
 บ  the group's first diz.  I was approached by a senior (I think he was at   บ
 บ  the time) of the group, Samuraion.  He said that if I did a .DIZ for the  บ
 บ  group, I'd become a member and have access to all their sites.  I wasn't  บ
 บ  all that excited, but it would have been a good chance to get my art      บ
 บ  skills up to par.                                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      So I went to another window, loaded up my ansi editor, and began to   บ
 บ  work on the diz.  Five minutes had passed and I had finished the diz.  I  บ
 บ  sent it over to Samuraion and he told me he liked it.  He gave me access  บ
 บ  to their channel, and told me that I would be added to the INFO as a      บ
 บ  member, and that I would soon have access to their site(s).  I was a      บ
 บ  little excited, thinking that this group would have a lot of success,     บ
 บ  and that I was a part of it (after all, without a diz, they wouldn't get  บ
 บ  far).  So I was given access, and soon became friends with a few people   บ
 บ  in the channel.                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      All was going good.  I was couriering their releases as soon as they  บ
 บ  were being released.  I was doing the job that their couriers should      บ
 บ  have been doing.  I was grabbing their releases off a member's shell      บ
 บ  account, and sending them all around my a/c, and to other sites which I   บ
 บ  wish to keep anonymous.                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I went into the channel a couple of days after the last release, and  บ
 บ  soon noticed after 5 minutes that I still had not been opped.  So I       บ
 บ  waited figuring I was lagged.  I waited, and waited, but still no +o.     บ
 บ  So I msged Acidplain, and he said he would go check the nfo file to see   บ
 บ  if I was in the group.  Turns out I wasn't in the latest nfo file, so he  บ
 บ  had no proof.  I told him that I was the one who did the DIZ for them,    บ
 บ  but still no ops.  I waited for Samuraion to come into the channel.  He   บ
 บ  came in about an hour after I first joined.  I told him that my ops had   บ
 บ  been taken away and that I was not in the NFO file.  He told me he added  บ
 บ  me, and said that he would do it again.  He sent me a copy of the latest  บ
 บ  one which had my name in it, and I kept it on my HD.  I joined the        บ
 บ  channel the next day, and to my surprise (yeah right), I was not given    บ
 บ  the ops.  I was added to the bot, and then got my ops back.  I was        บ
 บ  disconnected due to my computer freezing, and then connected back to IRC  บ
 บ  30 minsutes after.                                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I joined the channel again, and once again, no ops.  I was mad at     บ
 บ  this time, and so I sent a public message out stating that someone was    บ
 บ  removing my name out of the BOTS' list and that that was the reason for   บ
 บ  me not having my ops.                                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Samuraion joined the channel again, and he told me that he would      บ
 บ  once again add me to the bot.  I waited, and then had ops again.  I was   บ
 บ  then -o'ed and was wondering why.  I messaged Acidplain, and he said he   บ
 บ  didn't need me any longer because they had received a new diz and didn't  บ
 บ  want mine anymore.  I was fucking pissed (excuse the language).  So I     บ
 บ  left the channel, and msged X-Factor, and told him that Acidplain was     บ
 บ  asshole, and explained why I had called him that.  I got no reply, but    บ
 บ  when I joined channel #Legion, I was kicked out of the channel by none    บ
 บ  other than Acidplain.                                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I figured that whatever information I was giving to other members of  บ
 บ  the group, was being leaked out to Acidplain, so I said "Fuck This" and   บ
 บ  left the channel, never to return again.                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      So to all wondering if that interview contained some false            บ
 บ  information, none did whatsoever, whatever was said about Acidplain is    บ
 บ  true.  And I regret ever doing any work for that guy.  All respects go    บ
 บ  out to Samuraion for giving me a chance, and to X-Factor for being there  บ
 บ  when I needed help!                                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                               Signed,                      บ
 บ                                                  Storm Hacker              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ  networks.  There are at LEAST 20 of them, most real shitty with kiddoes   บ
 บ  on them who are learning to type.  So what's to do?  Most people don't    บ
 บ  even want to turn to the Internet here because they say it costs too      บ
 บ  much (my shell connection is 30$/month with 100 hours, not TOO bad but    บ
 บ  still I'd prefer if I didn't have my 4 megs quota).  This gets            บ
 บ  overcrowded boards, kiddoes (don't want to call them lamers since not     บ
 บ  all of them really are) who run them and who are saying "I want warez!    บ
 บ  I want messages!  I want the perfect board but I can't configure it!      บ

 บ  Dear RCN,                                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      This is a letter in reply to 'Da Phreak's' letter in RCN #22.  I      บ
 บ  really feel he should look harder into what he is talking about.  He      บ
 บ  asks :                                                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      "I mean, who is the thief here?  Us or them?  They charge $50 for a   บ
 บ  piece of plastic and some magnetic tape, and I AM THE CRIMINAL for        บ
 บ  getting it for free?"                                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Yes, my friend, you ARE the criminal.  Obviously he doesn't know how  บ
 บ  hard coding can be.  I'm sure he's unaware that it took iD YEARS to make  บ
 บ  quake the game it is and they should be rewarded.  This is why Mr. Law    บ
 บ  Making Guys have tried to protect these programmers from people like us.  บ
 บ  Later on, Da Phreak states:                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      "I mean, there is a chance <1 in 1 000 000 000> that I could          บ
 บ  randomly write binary that would replicate this last scene from a well    บ
 บ  known 3D game."                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Once again, his ignorance shines through!  Let's look at some very    บ
 บ  elementary probability:                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      (Let's assume 'this last scene from a well known 3D game' is 200k):   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      200x1024=204800 bytes                                                 บ
 บ      204800x8=1638400 bits                                                 บ
 บ      2^1638400= REALLY BIG.                                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      So you see, it's a bit bigger than 1 : 1 000 000 000.                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Now before someone calls me a hypocrite for saying all this, I'd      บ
 บ  just like to say that I accept how much work programmers put into their   บ
 บ  games.  I accept I'm a ciminal.  I just don't care. :-)                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                               Signed,                      บ
 บ                                                  Mr. Phallus               บ

 ฬออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออน
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Dear RCN,                                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      This letter is partly in response to Ermac's letter in RCN #21 about  บ
 บ  the benefits and popularity of IRC Couriering, and partly my opinions     บ
 บ  and other feelings about IRC Couriering.                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      IRC couriering, in my opinion at least, may show which files are the  บ
 บ  more popular ones, but with BBS trading (I don't do FTP trading), I know  บ
 บ  that you can find more online about the file you are going to download,   บ
 บ  as well as have a more reliable and faster connection to get the file     บ
 บ  from.  Often, when leeching off a DCC bot on IRC, you have to wait for a  บ
 บ  slot to become available, and when that does, how are you to know the     บ
 บ  bot won't drop connection while sending you the file.                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I know that when I BBS trade I can upload or download simulateously   บ
 บ  while knowing that I can get a connection on most multinode boards        บ
 บ  whenever I want, and know that the board is stable and won't disconnect   บ
 บ  in the middle of my transfer.  With IRC couriering also, you may be       บ
 บ  getting decent rates thru a t1 or t3 on your provider from the bot, but   บ
 บ  then, after it reaches your hd, you have to sit and wait while            บ
 บ  downloading it off your providers drive.  Now, this can be hasslesome,    บ
 บ  and I do know that many will go through this trouble just to get an 0     บ
 บ  day release, but it's not THAT beneficial timewise.                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Now, I don't want to sound like guys who setup DCC bots on IRC are    บ
 บ  lame, or stupid, I think that those who have bots steady going 24/7       บ
 บ  offering the latest files in any offer channel are very taleneted and     บ
 บ  should be commended.  I personally think though, that IRC Courering       บ
 บ  leaves the trading scene too simple.  I enjoy trading locally, and on     บ
 บ  occasional 800/888s, and I only use DCCs to get mags and small files      บ
 บ  (under 200k).  I enjoy the competition that trading gets on boards        บ
 บ  trying to beat other guys who have the same files.  IRC trading gievs     บ
 บ  people the "no ratio" advantage of taking files off IRC returning         บ
 บ  nothing, and then becoming well known.  I hope to start telnet trading    บ
 บ  soon, but right now I'm rebuilding my board from a hard drive crash, and  บ
 บ  don't have much time on my hands between that and work, so BBS trading    บ
 บ  is all I can do.                                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Finally, I'd like to address Ermac's saying that groups like          บ
 บ  Everlast and RiSC should get dcc channels and offer bots.  I personally   บ
 บ  would like to commend Everlast and RiSC and all other groups that only    บ
 บ  trade where the REAL competition is, on boards and sites.  Anyone can     บ
 บ  sit on IRC for a few hours a day offering some new files they DCCed from  บ
 บ  someone else, but it takes                                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      someone who is fairly talented to trade the fast files on the         บ
 บ  fastest boards and sites in the world.  Again, I don't think all DCC      บ
 บ  guys are bad, fATE did a good thing creating #fATEfiles, but it got way   บ
 บ  to popular and blown out of proprtion.  I have a lot of friends in fATE   บ
 บ  or who used to be in fATE, and have respect for the group itself.         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      In my area, I'm glad to see trading picking up because of IRC, but    บ
 บ  many people ask me why I don't just move my board to real fast, and       บ
 บ  leech off IRC all day.  The reason is, it's too easy.  Again, no          บ
 บ  competition and no ratios.  That's why sites and boards gain the          บ
 บ  importance they do.  Most TRUE traders get the files off the whq's or     บ
 บ  group affiliated sites, and spread from there.  IRC trading has been      บ
 บ  given too much importance in the scene.  IRC should be left as group      บ
 บ  channels to have group information publicly available, and in some        บ
 บ  cases, just a meeting place between fellow members to talk.               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                               Signed,                      บ
 บ                                                  King Cobra                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ฐ ฐฐ ฐ ฿ฐ ฐ฿ ฿ ฐ  ฿฿฿฿฿฿฿ ฐ ฐฐฐฐฐฐ ฐฐฐ

 ฿ฐ      ฿ฐ      ฿฿฿ฐ                                 ฿฿฿
      ฿                   ฿            a r t i c l e s !
                    ฐ฿                 ฐ฿
                     ฿                   ฿

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Rebel Chicken                                                 บ
 บ    Subject : Amnesia's Rebound?                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      It is always unfortunate to see a good establishment within the       บ
 บ  scene fall apart, and many are saying that Amnesia's future will not be   บ
 บ  much different from that of Malice, and thus, the scene assumes that      บ
 บ  Amnesia's peak has passed.  Those who curse Amensia predict that it will  บ
 บ  not last more than a few weeks after this recent "incident."  The         บ
 บ  incident to which I refer to took place a few days ago, and the incident  บ
 บ  describes Egoistic Fate's departure from Amnesia.  Egoistic Fate is the   บ
 บ  sysop of Malevolence, one of the world's fastest boards, if not the       บ
 บ  fastest.  Malevolence was the WHQ for Amnesia, and thus, Malevolence      บ
 บ  helped bring Amnesia much needed support from the BBS scene.  However,    บ
 บ  with Egoistic Fate's departure, two other senior traders, Erupt and       บ
 บ  Nytemyst, also quit Amnesia.                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      With senior members and HQs leaving left and right, the whole scene   บ
 บ  is saying that Amnesia's fall is near.  Will Amnesia remain a dominant    บ
 บ  courier force?  Is Amnesia REALLY doomed to fall?  To shed more light on  บ
 บ  the situation, RCN has granted them two interviews...                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ


                      r c n         
     ฿ฐ  ฿฿          ฿ ฐ      ฿฿ฐ            
    ฿฿฿  ฐ             ฿  ฿฿฿    ฿฿            
 ฐฐ  ฐฐ   ฐ ฿   ฿ฐ  ฐ฿฿   ฿   ฿ฐ  ฐฐฐ ฐ ฐ ฐ
         ฿฿฿฿฿฿  ฿  ฿฿฿฿฿฿      ฿
         ฿       ฿    ฿       ฿ ฿
    ฿  ฐ฿    ฿฿฿฿฿      ฿ ฐ    ฿฿฿฿฿   ฿฿    ฿ฐ฿
  ฿฿฿ฐ฿฿     ฿     ฿                       ฿฿฿
        ฿              i  n  t  e  r  v  i  e  w  s !

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Reporter : Rebel Chicken             Interviewee : Gahn                 บ
 บ    Subject  : Amnesia's Catch 22??      Affiliation : AMN BBS Coordinator  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Since you are the Amnesia BBS coordinator and the main force        บ
 บ        behind the Amnesia BBS team, you would know more about this than    บ
 บ        anyone.  How has Egoistic Fate's departure from Amnesia hurt the    บ
 บ        group?  After all, he ran the Amnesia WHQ, Malevolence, which       บ
 บ        happens to be one of the fastest boards in the world, if not THE    บ
 บ        fastest.                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ AMN: First off, Egoistic Fate's departure did not hurt Amnesia that      บ
 บ        much.  He told me he wanted to go RiSC about a week ago, I talked   บ
 บ        him out of it but I realized at that point that he was not loyal    บ
 บ        and only cared for his personal glory or something.  After hearing  บ
 บ        of this, we were already well on our way getting/looking for        บ
 บ        another WHQ anyway.                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: "Egoistic Fate's departure did not hurt Amnesia much," how could    บ
 บ        that be true?  When Egoistic Fate left Amnesia, he didn't leave by  บ
 บ        himself, he also took with him Erupt and Nytemyst, two of           บ
 บ        Amnesia's best couriers.                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ AMN: As far as Erupt and Nytemyst leaving, they are good friends of      บ
 บ        mine and I was a little upset that they did leave but I knew that   บ
 บ        their deparuter was coming too.  But let's face it, couriers can    บ
 บ        be replaced with a little time and effort, so the loss is not a     บ
 บ        great one.  The loss of the frienship hurts more then anything in   บ
 บ        this case.                                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Did you know at all that Egoistic Fate, Erupt, and Nytemyst were    บ
 บ        all planning to join Everlast after their departure from Amnesia?   บ
 บ        And if their departure was not so significant, why was an           บ
 บ        emergency meeting called in channel #Amnesia immediately following  บ
 บ        their departure?                                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ AMN: There was NO emergency meeting.  It was just to tell people what    บ
 บ        was going on so they know.  And no, I did not know they would       บ
 บ        choose to join Everlast.  It doesn't suprise me, but I did think    บ
 บ        that they would have chosen to join another courier group.  I       บ
 บ        thought that they might have gone independent because I was not     บ
 บ        aware that they had a liking for Everlast's leader, Mr. Skill, but  บ
 บ        I don't want to quote them at this point either.                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Which board is now the new Amnesia WHQ?                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ AMN: Well, Citadel Of Chaos is the new Amnesia WHQ.  It was a RiSC       บ
 บ        board but now it is an Amnesia board.  It has 8 nodes and its       บ
 บ        getting 2 telnets in a week and it's as fast if not faster then     บ
 บ        Malevolence.  You see, the problem with Marc's board was that       บ
 บ        Erupt and Nytemyst were the ONLY real uploaders there, so that to   บ
 บ        me is not an awesome bbs.  I liked it but I'm not concerned that    บ
 บ        this will affect us.  We are still business as usual in Amnesia.    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: When did Citadel of Chaos become an Amensia board, and when did it  บ
 บ        leave RiSC?                                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ AMN: Last week.                                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: As far as I know, isn't Citadel of Chaos located in Canada?  If     บ
 บ        so, is Amnesia switching its BBS efforts outside the US and toward  บ
 บ        Canada?                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ AMN: Why would we do that??  What is wrong with having a Canadian WHQ??  บ
 บ        You don't like Canadians??                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: No, I like Canada.  It was just a question, no need to be so PMS    บ
 บ        anal.                                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ AMN: I was kidding.  :)                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Are you aware of what Malevolence's position will be in Everlast?   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ AMN: Yes, Malevolence is now the Everlast Southern HQ or something.      บ
 บ        This should be interesting though.                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Southern HQ?  Why should this be interesting?  What more do you     บ
 บ        know about the situation?                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ AMN: Well, Marc HATES Third Son and hated it when Amnesia tried to       บ
 บ        support The Rock.  So I can't wait to see how he handles himself    บ
 บ        with Everlast.  I take that back, he does not HATE Third Son, he    บ
 บ        just HATES The Rock, Third Son's board.                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Isn't The Rock in the same area code as Malevolence?  Are they      บ
 บ        competing against each other?  Which courier group is The Rock      บ
 บ        affiliated with?                                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ AMN: The Rock is th Everlast WHQ.  Now if this is not the stupidist      บ
 บ        thing you ever heard of, what is??                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Well, it's not really stupid, but it is kind of strange to have     บ
 บ        two Everlast HQs located in the same area code.                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ AMN: Mr. Skill didn't need Malevolence, but for whatever reason, he had  บ
 บ        to have it.  I don't know what goes on in these people's heads,     บ
 บ        but well let me stop there.  I don't want to start flaming Mr.      บ
 บ        Skill or Everlast.  But whoever says Amnesia is going to die ONLY   บ
 บ        wishes it would because they were probably one of the ones that     บ
 บ        left or got kicked out of Amnesia at one point in time.  So you     บ
 บ        have to consider the source when you hear these things.  We are     บ
 บ        still on the TOP of the BBS scene.  And as far as Internet          บ
 บ        trading, I know our guys are really kicking some ass.  And look at  บ
 บ        this too, nobody else left Amnesia except for these three people.   บ
 บ        Life goes on, the scene has NO loyal people and that is just a      บ
 บ        fact of life.                                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

         ฿฿฿฿฿฿  ฿  ฿฿฿฿฿฿      ฿
         ฿       ฿    ฿       ฿ ฿
    ฿  ฐ฿    ฿฿฿฿฿      ฿ ฐ    ฿฿฿฿฿   ฿฿    ฿ฐ฿
  ฿฿฿ฐ฿฿     ฿     ฿                       ฿฿฿
        ฿              i  n  t  e  r  v  i  e  w  s !

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Reporter : Rebel Chicken             Interviewee : Ryu                  บ
 บ    Subject  : Ryu's Amnesia Site        Affiliation : Amnesia Siteop       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: A few weeks ago, MGD, an ex-Amnesia senior courier called it quits  บ
 บ        on Amnesia claiming that the group was going downhill.  He claimed  บ
 บ        that Amnesia was now a dead end and that its future was plagued     บ
 บ        with doom.  Do you believe that MGD's statements were made in good  บ
 บ        judgment?                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ AMN: Amnesia has been tagged with the image of a group going downhill.   บ
 บ        Most of this was done by people who are angry at Amnesia for some   บ
 บ        reason or another.  When MGD quit Amnesia, he didn't just quit and  บ
 บ        go to another group, he retired from the scene all together.  This  บ
 บ        should say something.  I personally don't think that Amnesia was    บ
 บ        the cause of it, but if he quit because Amnesia was going down      บ
 บ        hill, then why would he retire?  Why wouldn't he go to another      บ
 บ        trading group?  I don't think that Amnesia is a dead end at all.    บ
 บ        Many people have said that Amnesia is "going to die" and so they    บ
 บ        are leaving.  When these kind of rumors get spread, then people     บ
 บ        start leaving, and that in itself causes a group to be plagued      บ
 บ        with doom.  As for MGD, I think that there was a lot more involved  บ
 บ        than just that.                                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: MGD might not have gone to another courier group after he left      บ
 บ        Amnesia, but a lot of other Amnesia couriers are doing so right     บ
 บ        now.  Couriers are flooding out of Amnesia and joining RiSC.        บ
 บ        There are rumors that RiSC is planning to swallow up Amnesia piece  บ
 บ        by piece, and from the looks of it, it might seem to turn out to    บ
 บ        be happening even if RiSC did not plan it.                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ AMN: Rumors are the main thing here.  I have heard of several Amnesia    บ
 บ        couriers who were going to RiSC.  After talking to them, I found    บ
 บ        out that most of them were not leaving, but just wanted to be       บ
 บ        heard.  Or perhaps the rumors were started by someone trying to     บ
 บ        take down Amnesia.  I have also heard about RiSC planning on        บ
 บ        swallowing up Amnesia.  I do not believe them.  Some couriers will  บ
 บ        leave Amnesia and go to other courier groups, but Amnesia will      บ
 บ        gain new couriers to replace them.  For instance, Vile and          บ
 บ        Revolver from RTS recently joined Amnesia.  With more additions to  บ
 บ        the trading team, Amnesia can and will replace anyone lost to       บ
 บ        RiSC.                                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: From what you're saying, it might sound like any courier is         บ
 บ        replaceable.  Like, if an Amnesia courier dropped dead, nobody      บ
 บ        would really care.  But if RiSC is planning to swallow up Amnesia,  บ
 บ        RiSC would be doing so by swallowing up Amnesia sites first since   บ
 บ        sites are NOT so easily replaceable.  I've been informed that you   บ
 บ        run a site for Amnesia, and for purposes of keeping that site       บ
 บ        anonymous, we shall refer to your site as The Donut Hole for the    บ
 บ        remainder of the interview.  Is it true that RiSC offered you a     บ
 บ        position in RiSC as a siteop?  Were they trying to swallow you out  บ
 บ        of Amnesia?  From the looks of it, you probably refused RiSC's      บ
 บ        invitation, and if so, why?                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ AMN: That is a good question.  I don't know if RiSC was trying to        บ
 บ        "swallow" Amnesias' sites when they offered my site, The Donut      บ
 บ        Hole, a position in RiSC.  RiSC couldn't care less about me, they   บ
 บ        just wanted the site.  That is the reason that I decided to stay    บ
 บ        with Amnesia.  When I was talking to a RiSC senior about the site   บ
 บ        coming to RiSC, he mentioned that my co-siteop would be coming      บ
 บ        with me.  Later I found out from two other reliable sources that    บ
 บ        they were planning on dumping my co-siteops as soon as I was in     บ
 บ        the door.  I did not like this, since the co-siteops on my site     บ
 บ        put in a lot of hard work and effort to make it what it was.  That  บ
 บ        is why I decided not to go with RiSC.                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Who was that RiSC senior you were talking to?  And who were these   บ
 บ        two reliable resources?  Were your two informers RiSC members who   บ
 บ        could not stand to see you cheated?  You can call me psychic, but   บ
 บ        I have a strong feeling this RiSC senior who was planning to cheat  บ
 บ        you might be Eagle 1 since the other 2 out of the 3 RiSC seniors    บ
 บ        are not currently active.  Also, would one of your two informers    บ
 บ        be Lurch?  I was informed that Lurch was recently kicked out of     บ
 บ        RiSC for doing something wrong.  Perhaps he was kicked out of RiSC  บ
 บ        because he was informing you that you were about to be cheated?     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ AMN: Well, the senior that I was talking to was Darkside.  As for my     บ
 บ        other two reliable sources, I can't tell you who they were, as I    บ
 บ        gave my word that they would remain anonymous.  As for Lurch, I     บ
 บ        have no idea why he is no longer in RiSC, although I do know that   บ
 บ        it had nothing to do with me or my site.                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Oh, dam, I guess I'm not psychic then.  Oh darn.                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ AMN: Heheheheee... you put 2 and 2 together and you got 4.               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Also, I might not be a good judge for this, but from word of        บ
 บ        mouth, your site seems to be the only site left in Amnesia that's   บ
 บ        any good.  Without your site, people would say that Amnesia would   บ
 บ        REALLY turn to shit since Amnesia couriers would have no where to   บ
 บ        upload to.  From the looks of it, Amnesia might turn out to be a    บ
 บ        another dead Malice.  Are there any other good sites left in        บ
 บ        Amnesia worthy to be called a GOOD site?  After all, BBX, one of    บ
 บ        Amnesia's fastest sites recently left for RiSC.  You might turn     บ
 บ        out to be the only loyal Amnesia siteop.                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ AMN: Well, BBX is a good site and losing it to RiSC did hurt, but        บ
 บ        Amnesia still has at least 5 to 6 good sites as well as a courier   บ
 บ        base for the couriers to trade off of.  Amnesia has rocked the      บ
 บ        European courier scene for a long time and will continue to do so,  บ
 บ        this should say something about their Internet power.  As for me    บ
 บ        being the only loyal siteop left, I doubt that.  Amnesia has quite  บ
 บ        a few loyal people onboard.                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: That's good to hear, nobody likes to see a strong organization die  บ
 บ        out.  A few weeks ago, another strong European courier group        บ
 บ        called Rapier unfortunately disbanded because Rom Racer, Rapier's   บ
 บ        leader who also happens to be a Razor 1911 coordinator, no longer   บ
 บ        had time to manage the group.  Many of Rapiers' top couriers moved  บ
 บ        over to Everlast, however, I have not received word that any good   บ
 บ        Rapier couriers moved over to Amnesia.  Did Rapier's death help     บ
 บ        Amnesia at all?                                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ AMN: I can't say if Rapier's death was good or bad for Amnesia.          บ
 บ        Whenever a group dies, it forces the members to move to another     บ
 บ        group.  Amnesia picked up Rainbow and Skuzzi from Rapier, and they  บ
 บ        have both worked out very well.                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Reporter : Rebel Chicken             Interviewee : Jester King          บ
 บ    Subject  : ex-Razor Member           Affiliation : Canned Outta Razor   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: I have heard rumors that you were kicked out of Razor 1911 for one  บ
 บ        reason or another, but no one would really talk about it.  How and  บ
 บ        why were you kicked out of Razor?                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ JST: It was a big surprise to me, I was not notified of being kicked     บ
 บ        out of Razor even though I have been one of the longest remaining   บ
 บ        members to the team.  I just simply downloaded the latest release   บ
 บ        of 3 weeks ago, Front Page Sports Baseball, the big 56 disk non     บ
 บ        working game, and noticed myself erased off the razor.nfo file.     บ
 บ        Rumor has it I was kicked out of Razor after being considered       บ
 บ        worthless to the team.  I don't take that lightly, "HELLO SPEED     บ
 บ        RACER, WHO TAUGHT YOU HOW TO MAKE CARDS, AND SETUP CONFERENCES,     บ
 บ        WHO SUPPLIED YOU ME AND NOBODY ELSE!"                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: How long were you a part of Razor?  Were you in any other games     บ
 บ        groups before you were a part of Razor?                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ JST: I started as a member of The Firm, 6 years ago I believe.  I was a  บ
 บ        card supplier for Wilkins, an old school German guy!  One day, TSR  บ
 บ        (The Speed Racer) called me when he was simply a member of NEXUS    บ
 บ        asking me if I would join and supply him cards.  Cards were gotten  บ
 บ        differently back then, it was during the Killerette/Phonestud &     บ
 บ        Maximillion card supplying spree, TSR had no connections to         บ
 บ        getting cards.  I have been members of The Firm, CMS, Nexus,        บ
 บ        Tdu-Jam!, Hybrid, PWA, Scum, Phoenix, Tyranny, Raw Meggage, RiSC    บ
 บ        and probably a whole lot of smaller groups too.  Oh, and I was in   บ
 บ        DOD too.                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Ever since Nexus merged into Razor, I have always sided with TSR,   บ
 บ        even when Razor was being taken over by TRC (The Renegade           บ
 บ        Chemist).  But I respect TRC much more than TSR, and my personal    บ
 บ        friend Randall Flagg, who taught me a lot about the scene!  I have  บ
 บ        no respect for TSR anymore.                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ JST: According to Druidkin, the Razor Internet Coordinator, you were     บ
 บ        kicked out of Razor because you attempted to pull a "coup d'etat."  บ
 บ        He informed me that you tried to kick out the current Razor         บ
 บ        leaders, and with Tklp's help, you were planning to make yourself   บ
 บ        the new Razor leader, and Tklp a Razor senior.  Is that true?       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Druidkin is not a friend of mine, but he could only say what he     บ
 บ        knows.  I did consider taking over Razor but that was after being   บ
 บ        kicked out of the group!  And if I had the time to do it I would,   บ
 บ        it would be a success too!  I did consider kicking out 90% of the   บ
 บ        group and leaving maybe 10 members.  TSR did it, my turn sounded    บ
 บ        like a good idea.  The only person in the group who I respect is    บ
 บ        Pharaoh.  I needed some suppliers to help, and since my plans       บ
 บ        wouldn't be to attack Prestige, I wouldn't have considered to try   บ
 บ        and take Prestige suppliers.  Tklp, although immature, is a nice    บ
 บ        guy.  He's new to the scene and I usually hate newbies, but he is   บ
 บ        an exception.  Most of my contacts are retired, but Razor should    บ
 บ        be run as a small group, no more than 15 people, and no couriers,   บ
 บ        all members.                                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ JST: But Druidkin said that you were kicked out BECAUSE you were trying  บ
 บ        to takeover Razor.  And you're saying that you tried to takeover    บ
 บ        BECAUSE you were kicked out.  Somebody is lying.                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Well, it wouldn't make sense to takeover a group while I'm still    บ
 บ        in right?  If that was the case, I would just lay back like I was,  บ
 บ        and wait until the smoke cleared.                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ JST: What are your current plans for yourself in the scene.  Have you    บ
 บ        joined any other games groups or perhaps have you started your own  บ

 บ        to be.  I even thought of returning the group to its rightful       บ

 บ    Reporter : Rebel Chicken             Interviewee : Stank-e              บ
 บ    Subject  : Core Leader               Affiliation : Pretty Smart...      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: There are tons of new courier groups that pop up each week, and     บ
 บ        many of them don't live past that very same week.  However, every   บ
 บ        now and then, one of these new courier groups do make it up there   บ
 บ        with the older groups.  For example, I've seen that Core, your      บ
 บ        courier group, has been doing very well lately, and that your       บ
 บ        offer channel #Phatfiles is packed with offerers all the time, and  บ
 บ        some could say that your channel is now better than channel         บ
 บ        #M8leech which has been around for months, and that channel         บ
 บ        #Phatfiles will soon be more popular than channel #Exceed.  What    บ
 บ        has contributed to its success?                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ COR: Well, we started out small trying to do the things we could.        บ
 บ        Offering in channel #M8leech and #Exceed talking about our channel  บ
 บ        and after doing that long enough, we got some attention.  So then   บ
 บ        we asked for other groups to join in and help us like NGT, GCD,     บ
 บ        and then WWW the people who ran the old channel #Leech.  We all     บ
 บ        merged into #Phatfiles and that's what has given us more offerers   บ
 บ        than other channels because of #Phatfiles is like a home to a       บ
 บ        couple of smaller courier groups.                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: So channel #Phatfiles is not a product of Core?  I always see Core  บ
 บ        couriers offering in there, so I always assumed that the channel    บ
 บ        is run by Core.  If Core does not own channel #Phatfiles, then      บ
 บ        which courier group does own it, or are you saying that a bunch of  บ
 บ        smaller groups run it?  Even so, smaller groups look at the         บ
 บ        biggest of the small groups as their leader, so which courier       บ
 บ        group is the most dominant in channel #Phatfiles?                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ COR: As it started of Palm who was running #M8leech for a while started  บ
 บ        out #Phatfiles and since he was in our group we joined and helped   บ
 บ        him.  So Core does run the channel and when Palm is out, I help     บ
 บ        run it.                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: I've heard rumors that inside Core, there's a new Core IRC Team     บ
 บ        concept that is being organized as we speak that is meant to        บ
 บ        revolutionize the scene.  I've not been told of the details of      บ
 บ        this "Core IRC Team," but from what I know so far, it seems to be   บ
 บ        pretty interesting.  Are the rumors true, is there such a Core IRC  บ
 บ        Team on the drawing boards?                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ COR: As of now, the Core IRC Team is still in the works.  You can see    บ
 บ        it sometimes in #Phatfiles but not the way we want it.  My idea is  บ
 บ        to get all of our IRC couriers together and have certain teams      บ
 บ        offer different kinds of warez.  Like team 1 will offer 0 day and   บ
 บ        team 2 will take graphic programs.  And we want to have 5 to 10     บ
 บ        bots on 24/7 offering the latest and the greatest files.  And we    บ
 บ        want to become #1 on IRC and think we can achieve easily, if we     บ
 บ        work for it.                                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: But all of the other courier groups have such offering teams as     บ
 บ        well right?  How will Core be able to sustain 5 to 10 bots          บ
 บ        offering 24/7?  Is that 5 to 10 bots per team?  How many offerers   บ
 บ        make up one team?                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ COR: As I have seen, this is a totally new conecept which will make      บ
 บ        exchanging files over IRC easier, at least through Core.  We are    บ
 บ        going for 5 to 10 on each team so there will be a lot of offerers.  บ
 บ        At first, we won't be full strength but once we achieve 5 to 10 on  บ
 บ        each team, we will definitely be #1 on the list.                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Your Core IRC Team concept would definitely be of help to the       บ
 บ        masses, but I'm sure that other courier groups will get jealous,    บ
 บ        and in the process, they'll start colliding the fuck out of your    บ
 บ        offerers.  Have you taken prevention methods to secure your bots,   บ
 บ        so they do offer 24/7 and not just 10 minutes after they're loaded  บ
 บ        up?                                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ COR: Thats where I come in.  I have been offering on IRC for a while     บ
 บ        and I'm going to make sure that the people who offer make there     บ
 บ        bots stable so they don't eof or excess flood.  As for colliding    บ
 บ        goes, I don't think anyone in the bigger groups would try to        บ
 บ        collide us just because they are jealous.  If this does come        บ
 บ        about, we will take measures to keep our bots up.  Maybe it'll      บ
 บ        just cause us to offer more!                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: A good offering group is still, only an offering group, and not a   บ
 บ        courier group.  A good courier group always has a good source of    บ
 บ        ftp sites where the offerers can leech off of.  Does Core have      บ
 บ        this resource in sites as well?                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ COR: Well as sites go my other half, Edge, who is working on that as I   บ
 บ        work on IRC.  We are on a few large sites along with other large    บ
 บ        groups.  But as everyone knows, everyone can always use more good   บ
 บ        sites.  It's give and take, the more FTP sites we have the more we  บ
 บ        can offer on IRC.                                                   บ

 บ    Reporter : Dr. Conway                Interviewee : Sweet                บ
 บ    Subject  : AOL Couriering            Affiliation : UPS/UPSS             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      UPS is a couriering group that is based on AOL.  They get about 50%   บ
 บ  of the releases by quality groups like Razor, Hybrid, DOD and Napalm to   บ
 บ  thousands of people using AOL.  What is exceptional about this group is   บ
 บ  that there is no "I am the k-RaDDeSt here, BoW to mE!!" attidude so       บ
 บ  commonly found in AOL groups, and the releases that they send out are     บ
 บ  all working, and always clearly labeled with a NFO from the group that    บ
 บ  released the ware, and usually a NFO from the UPS member that actually    บ
 บ  TESTED the release before uploading it.  UPS is recognized on AOL to be   บ
 บ  the elite without a doubt.  They embody an AOL "legend" since they have   บ
 บ  been around on AOL much longer then any of their competitors.             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Following is an interview with Sweet, a Coucil member of UPS, and     บ
 บ  also the President of UPSS - the "training corps" for UPS.  While UPS is  บ
 บ  concerned with the couriering the warez until they get to AOL, UPSS       บ
 บ  helps spread releases on AOL.                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Can you describe the recent activity of UPS and some statistics on  บ
 บ        UPS such as the number of uploads a week, etc?                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ UPS: Sure can.  Well, we're hitting 2 gigs a week uploading and our      บ
 บ        MMing crew (UPSS) is getting it out very much on AOL.  So we're     บ
 บ        very busy.                                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Well, of course you can't count how many gigs were "couriered" on   บ
 บ        AOL, but how many MM's a day does UPSS deliver?                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ UPS: Well, we keep track of them now so we're MMing anywhere from 20k    บ
 บ        to 30k a day, and by a day, I mean regular busy hours on AOL and    บ
 บ        that's thousand of files!                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Cool!  How many members does UPS have curretly?                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ UPS: Around 60 right now, that includes our UPSS, since UPSS is just a   บ
 บ        "training" corps for UPS, and they have 20 members.                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Can you give me a little brief history of UPS?                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ UPS: Sure.  I love to listen to old skewlers talk on IRC.  We were a     บ
 บ        year old on July 4th.  Welp, basically, UPS really started a year   บ
 บ        and a half ago and it broke up after a few months because the guys  บ
 บ        lost interest and got busy in the real world and stuff, and then    บ
 บ        last year on July 4th, Nun, Deathwish, and WeX started it back up   บ
 บ        again with Phun, Trubl, and some of the other guys that I don't     บ
 บ        know.  Then, they started UPSS about six or seven months ago as a   บ
 บ        training corps.  They wanted to do ACCURATE fresh uploads and then  บ
 บ        MM the AOL.  So now here we are bigger and better.                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Cool.  Can you tell me why UPS hung on for more than a year now     บ
 บ        whereas other groups on AOL form and break within a few weeks?      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ UPS: Yes I can.  Because we are very very tight for a group on the IRC   บ
 บ        or even for an AOL based group.                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Can you elaborate on "tight?"                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ UPS: We're very tight and we all work our asses off.  Our uploaders are  บ
 บ        GOOD, fast, and knowledgeable.  Our MMers are good, fast, and       บ
 บ        knowledgeable.  Well, most of us talk voice all the time, some, if  บ
 บ        not most of us, have met in the real world.  We communicate all     บ
 บ        the time.  We have very STRICT rules for uploading and couriering.  บ
 บ        We follow a very STRICT chain of command and we keep or try to      บ
 บ        keep the bullshit outta the way of our job.                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Do you compete directly with any Internet based groups?             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ UPS: No, we don't compete with any Internet based groups.  We're a       บ
 บ        different type of group.                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Do you use FTP sites or IRC for couriering?                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ UPS: Well, we use FTP sites and our own private site.  We got Internet   บ
 บ        group people who courier to our sites after they do for their own   บ
 บ        groups.                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: You mean people from other groups?                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ UPS: Yup, AFTER is the keyword here, though.                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Do you have any serious competition from any AOL groups?            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ UPS: I guess as far as AOL goes?  Nope, honestly we don't because UPSS   บ
 บ        is so kicking.  We're in every room all the time.  I don't know of  บ
 บ        any other group that has such a WELL organized MMing group like we  บ
 บ        do.  But I'm the President of UPSS, so I'm kinda prejudiced, ok?    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: I understand.  What about Dogz?                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ UPS: Dogz?  Hehe... well, a good way to judge which group is getting it  บ
 บ        out to the AOLers, is to get on some MMs and see what the MMers     บ
 บ        got in their boxes.  I do that all the time.  It's usually better   บ
 บ        than 50% UPS files.  Enough said.                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: You're right there.  UPS does have the majority of the mailz.  Do   บ
 บ        you have any affiliations with releasing groups such as Razor,      บ
 บ        DOD, Hybrid, etc?                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ UPS: We do not.  We have had in the past, but, like, the stigma of AOL   บ
 บ        and the fear of Internet groups has stopped releasing groups from   บ
 บ        letting us become official.                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      UPS does not have any affiliations with any releasing groups at the   บ
 บ  moment, but I haven't seen one worthwhile (or worthless) ware in the      บ
 บ  past year that hasn't been on AOL in a matter of hours after it's         บ
 บ  released by the major groups.  Judge for yourselves...                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
