 บ    Reporter : Glycerine                 Interviewee : Tklp                 บ
 บ    Subject  : Hi, I'm Tklp.             Affiliation : ROR?                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      The following is an interview that Rebel Chicken forgot publish in    บ
 บ  RCN a few issues back.  It might be a little outdated, so give it a few   บ
 บ  weeks lag, and don't laugh too hard at what Tklp has to say...            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Would you mind stating who you are, and what affiliations you       บ
 บ        presently hold?                                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ ROR: My nickname is Tklp, and I'm the leader of ROR (Release on          บ
 บ        Rampage), Malice, Mortality, and Sodom.                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Now, you may have read in RCN an interview that was conducted by    บ
 บ        an anonymous scene member to a member of iD Software.  This         บ
 บ        interview said that due to your supposed release of QUAKE FINAL,    บ
 บ        you may be in some serious trouble.  What do you have to say about  บ
 บ        this?                                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ ROR: That iD can lick my balls and they can phear me.  They announced    บ
 บ        on Eyewitness News on CBS that I released it, and no one had said   บ
 บ        shit to me nor do they have any evidence of who I am, so fuck 'em.  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: CBS News!  Wow man!  That's Krazy You Little Punk, no pun           บ
 บ        intended...                                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ ROR: :)                                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Now, there have been rumors about how the release of QUAKE was a    บ
 บ        fake and how it was only the BETA.  Would you mind clarifying this  บ
 บ        for all the readers?                                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ ROR: It's not a beta, however it's not the final.  It turned out to be   บ
 บ        the pre-release final, the only thing missing is modem play.  We    บ
 บ        apologize for anyone who is disapointed, although the feedback      บ
 บ        from the release has been 95% great...                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Yes.  It is a great game.  I haven't played it myself but I've      บ
 บ        seen it at a friends.  Anyways, there was a patch for the modem     บ
 บ        play released by THC.  Now would you say that this PATCH is the     บ
 บ        key that turns the PRE-RELEASE to the FINAL?                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ ROR: I really couldn't say, because who knows, iD might make a drastic   บ
 บ        change, but I doubt it.                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: There is also some rumor going around that the FINAL DOOM released  บ
 บ        by Razor 1911 is the actual QUAKE final, do you have any comments   บ
 บ        on this issue?                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ ROR: Hahahaah!  Whoever said that is a complete dumbass, Final Doom is   บ
 บ        just something GT Interactive made, it's a bunch of new levels for  บ
 บ        DOOM 2 with a dumb new story line.                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Would you say this is just another LAME release to keep a group     บ
 บ        alive?  If not, would you have released it if you had a chance?     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ ROR: No no, FINAL DOOM is a very awaited title, and yes I would have     บ
 บ        released it.  It's just that I think DOOM 2 has had it's time, and  บ
 บ        new WADS just don't entertain me.                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: I agree with you.  DOOM WADS are getting tiring and lame.           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ ROR: Another issue I would like to talk to you about is about the        บ
 บ        information that was released in RCN about you.  Do you have        บ
 บ        anything to say about this?                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Not really, the only thing correct is my city and state.            บ
 บ        Everything else is total wack.                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ ROR: So you are not afraid of being busted or of being flamed by scene   บ
 บ        members who dislike you?                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Nope.                                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ ROR: Well, I would just like to say GOOD LUCK in the future with ROR.    บ
 บ        I think it's a great team, and have always respected it and it's    บ
 บ        members.  Good Luck man!  Do you have any last words you would      บ
 บ        like to say to members?                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Well, I'd like to greet a lot of people, but I'm afraid if I do     บ
 บ        greet a bunch of people I might leave out some of my friends that   บ
 บ        didn't cross my mind and I don't want to hurt anyone.               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ ROR: Hehe... any disses?                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Nah, I'm done with my life in scene controversy.                    บ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Krypto                                                        บ
 บ    Subject : Soft Wars : Companies Strike Back?                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      In the pirate's never ending battle with each other to supply and     บ
 บ  courier software, there is a common enemy.  In their end of the war,      บ
 บ  software companies develops software of massive size, imposes high        บ
 บ  fines, and will use whatever it is at their disposal to stop you from     บ
 บ  spreading their software.  But how effective are they?  And who is truly  บ
 บ  winning the war?                                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Although, most software developers write programs that hog storage    บ
 บ  resources to allow them less limitations and perhaps develop better       บ
 บ  software.  There is no denial that larger programs are harder to pirate   บ
 บ  and is discouraging to even pirate.  From 1988, software programs were    บ
 บ  averaging the mere size of 2 megabytes, while today has grown to about    บ
 บ  650 megabytes on a single CD.  Today, 650 megabytes is a lot relative to  บ
 บ  2.0 megabytes, but how effective has this growth in size slowed down      บ
 บ  software piracy?  Through the help of the hardware industry, in           บ
 บ  particular modem development, and skilled software crackers/rippers, one  บ
 บ  sees that software pirates are NOT spending a more significant amount of  บ
 บ  time transferring programs from computer to computer.  In the period of   บ
 บ  1988, the most predominant modulator/demodulators (modems) were going at  บ
 บ  speeds of 2400 bytes per second. By doing your math correctly, it would   บ
 บ  say that one would spend about 2 hours and 19 minutes per transfer of     บ
 บ  programs.                                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Through CD ripping, today pirates are able to cut down programs to    บ
 บ  approximately 28.0 megabytes (some of the more successful rips average    บ
 บ  about 12.0 megabytes).  As most home pirates don't have ISDN lines, they  บ
 บ  are limited to modems running at 33.6 kilobytes per second modems.  Once  บ
 บ  again, by doing your math it shows that software pirates are spending     บ
 บ  about the same 2 hours and 19 minutes transferring programs today as      บ
 บ  they did over 8 years ago.  Through statistics, it shows that this has    บ
 บ  been a slightly fluctuating trend.  So although today's pirates maybe     บ
 บ  using t1 lines or even t3s on their Internet service providers, pirates   บ
 บ  are limited to this 2:19 barrier when transferring files to their home    บ
 บ  PC.                                                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Modem Speeds as a Function of Time :                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ   +48ษอออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป   บ
 บ      บ                                                             บ   บ

 บ  1:00วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ   บ
 บ      บ                                         บ   บ
 บ      วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ   บ
 บ      บ                                         บ   บ
 บ  0:30วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ   บ
 บ      บ                                         บ   บ
 บ      วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ   บ
 บ      บ                                         บ   บ
 บ     ศอออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ   บ
 บ    ณ   1988      1990      1992      1994      1996      1996 (56k ISDN)   บ
 บ    ณ                                  Time (Year)                          บ
 บ    ภฤ  Time Spent Transferring Programs (Hours)                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Perhaps because Moore's Law states that technology doubles every 16   บ
 บ  months, transfer rates have also gone up to match the increasing size of  บ
 บ  software programs.  CDs however, still limits software pirates against    บ
 บ  video intensive software such as Phantasmagoria by Sierra Online.  In     บ
 บ  any case, my analysis shows that use of CDs as the predominant choice of  บ
 บ  media is by no means an efficient means of preventing software piracy.    บ
 บ  Although the use of CDs does not by any means efficiently stop us from    บ
 บ  pirating, we must also consider that most of the software pirates         บ
 บ  releasing software under an affiliation can be considered professionals.  บ
 บ  Most pirating laymen, who classically copied computer disks and gave      บ
 บ  them to friends, are unable to crack and rip CDs themselves.  Thus        บ
 บ  rendering CDs unpiratable to that specific class of computer users.  To   บ
 บ  the other extreme, there are those who burn CDs, and can produce mass     บ
 บ  quantities of illegally pirated software.  This once again shows the      บ
 บ  ineffectiveness of CDs as an anti-piracy measure.                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Another measure in prevention of software piracy taken on by the      บ
 บ  software publishers is the use of some kind of documentation or serial    บ
 บ  number check.  Again, to the pirating laymen, this is an effective        บ
 บ  prevention of piracy.  However, it doesn't take much to photocopy the     บ
 บ  documentation from a friend nor is it hard to write down the serial       บ
 บ  number while you're at a friend's house while copying those disks.  To    บ
 บ  the professional pirates, these documentation checks are only a small     บ
 บ  obstacle in their attempt to illegally reproduce the software which is    บ
 บ  useable to others.  Skilled programmers and crackers can easily render    บ
 บ  most software checks inoperable and determine the proper serial number    บ
 บ  for the software.                                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      This inability to prevent software pirates from illegally             บ
 บ  reproducing their software is definitely an indication that software      บ
 บ  pirates are winning the battle against software publishers.  According    บ
 บ  to a May 1995 Computerworld survey of information systems professionals,  บ
 บ  47% of the respondents admitted to copying commercial software            บ
 บ  illegally, despite the fact that 78% agreed it should never be done.      บ
 บ  Should this statement be true, it would further back up the statement     บ
 บ  that the computer software publishers are losing the battle against       บ
 บ  software piracy.  Here are some figures that the BSA (Business Software   บ
 บ  Alliance) are trying to convince people to believe.                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Software piracy costs the industry :                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      $482 every second                                                     บ
 บ      $28,900 every minute                                                  บ
 บ      $1.7 million every hour                                               บ
 บ      $41.6 million every day                                               บ
 บ      $291.5 million every week                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      In an attempt to determine what some major software                   บ
 บ  developers/publishers have to say about the issues discussed in this      บ
 บ  article, I sent them the following email :                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Hello my name is Douglas Watts. I am a writer at Reality Check        บ
 บ  Network, which is an electronic based magazine.  I am currently writing   บ
 บ  an article about software piracy, and how the software industries are     บ
 บ  fighting it.  I would like to take a moment of your time to ask you a     บ
 บ  few questions on behalf of your company.                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      With the increasing use of CD-ROMs by consumers and developers, it    บ
 บ  has allowed the developers to put more information in programs with less  บ
 บ  storage limitations.  From your company's stand point, how has the        บ
 บ  increasing use of CD-ROMs dampened software piracy?                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      In the battle against software piracy, what measures has your         บ
 บ  company taken to PREVENT piracy of their products?                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      From your company's view, how has the software industry been faring   บ
 บ  against the battle against piracy?                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Your information such as your name and position at the company would  บ
 บ  be greatly appreciated.  Thank you for your time and patience with this   บ
 บ  matter.                                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                               Signed,                      บ
 บ                                                  Douglas Watts             บ
 บ                                                  Reality Check Network     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I had written this letter to IBM, Microsoft, iD Software, Symantec,   บ
 บ  and Netscape.  The response to this was staggering, as none of them       บ
 บ  replied anytime before this article was published.  Perhaps this shows    บ
 บ  the concern that these companies have toward software piracy?  We'll      บ
 บ  never really know.                                                        บ

 บ  ณ We're sorry to interrupt your playing of some crappy racing game that   บ
 บ  ณ just got released, but we thought we'd bring you the new incarnation    บ
 บ  ณ of the game that revolutionized computer golf back in the day.  This    บ
 บ  ณ superb title blends stunning graphics and exquisite gameplay to create  บ
 บ  ณ a realistic golfing experience.  You'll think that you're on the        บ
 บ  ณ green, as you play with Arnold Palmer, a living legend in the game of   บ
 บ  ณ golf.                                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      We're sorry to interrupt your playing of some stupid ass golf game.   บ
 บ  The game I'm referring to is "Links Legends In Sports '97 (c) Access"     บ
 บ  released by Prestige on July 18, 1996.  Why is this release any           บ
 บ  different from the myriad of other Prestige releases?  Well, this         บ
 บ  release sucked because it was horribly ripped.  Nowhere in the            บ
 บ  prestige.nfo does Prestige inform its downloaders that this game only     บ
 บ  includes ONE of the available FOUR golfers.  Nowhere in the prestige.nfo  บ
 บ  does Prestige inform its downloaders that all modem and Win95 support     บ
 บ  was ripped out.  All in all, this was a horrible rip because Prestige     บ
 บ  should never have been so sloppy as to release only 1/4th of the game.    บ
 บ  But to make matters worse, Prestige also did a horrible packaging job by  บ
 บ  not informing people the fact that they were only downloading a portion   บ
 บ  of the game.  So to all those who downloaded it, sorry about the big      บ
 บ  surprise, if you're mad at the crap you downloaded, blame the group that  บ
 บ  released the crap.                                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      To make matters worse, Prestige starts off this release by putting    บ
 บ  down a more established games group, Razor 1911.  The "playing of some    บ
 บ  crappy racing game" that Prestige was referring to in the prestige.nfo    บ
 บ  was Razor's release of Grand Prix 2.  Prestige had no right to put down   บ
 บ  Razor for that release.  First off, Razor did not just release the game   บ
 บ  with one car available for you to drive, nor did Razor release the game   บ
 บ  with but one track to drive on.  If anything, Prestige should have been   บ
 บ  congratulating Razor for beating them on this release, but instead, all   บ
 บ  we hear is Prestige crying "SOUR GRAPES."                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      To make matters even worse, Prestige decided to give their release a  บ
 บ  fat 100% game rating.  Excuse me, but if I've never gotten 100% on a      บ
 บ  test when answering only 1/4 of the questions, and believe me, I've       บ
 บ  taken A LOT of tests.  So, if Prestige has some kind of weird fucking     บ
 บ  new counting method, I'd be glad to learn.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      1, 2, 8, 5, 10, A, B, 4...                                            บ

 บ    Author  : Traveler                                                      บ
 บ    Subject : A Revolution in IRCii Scripting                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      As a former IRC courier, I know one of the most annoying parts is     บ
 บ  dealing with buggy, slow, and ugly scripts.  I remember the hours of      บ
 บ  download and setup time, just to have the script go completely nuts       บ
 บ  after 20 minutes in channel #fATEfiles.  Now, there is an alternative.    บ
 บ  Atlantis combines the ease of fphoenix, the protection of LiCe, and the   บ
 บ  speed of Tech5.  Unlike many others however, Atlantis also comes with     บ
 บ  its own array of unique features that makes it the most powerful IRC      บ
 บ  couriering tool around.                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      First, let me point out the main advantage of Atlantis : DCC RESUME.  บ
 บ  This is the first IRCii script EVER to incorperate this breakthrough.     บ
 บ  Atlantis DCC RESUME allows not only leeway in how big you make the pack   บ
 บ  to offer, allowing more pack spaces, it completely erradicates any time   บ
 บ  wasted resending entire packs to those who's client died for some         บ
 บ  reason.  Resume, however, is just one of the many XDCC features offered   บ
 บ  by Atlantis.  Ever since fphoenix introduced queuing, we've all been      บ
 บ  plagued by its inadequacy.  I'm sure all of you have gotten stuck on      บ
 บ  queues that never send.  Not only that, they keep annoying you with       บ
 บ  notices of your queue possition that never changes.  With Atlantis, this  บ
 บ  ends.  Atlantis has the fastest queuing around that is totally            บ
 บ  unexploitable, and bug free.  Some of the other XDCC options you'll find  บ
 บ  in Atlantis include : secured DCC, quick save of pack lists, and delayed  บ
 บ  auto pack listing.                                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      For those of you looking for a script that has more than just fancy   บ
 บ  XDCC options, Atlantis will prove more than enough for you.  Atlantis     บ
 บ  offers many setup options, from kick/logoff msg's, to channel flood       บ
 บ  sensor settings that allow you to control most of the idiots testing      บ
 บ  their neato new nick floods.  With Atlantis you'll never have to worry    บ
 บ  about being vulnerable.  There are 4 flood protection settings ranging    บ
 บ  from totally open to totally cloaked.  Not to mention, DCC exploit        บ
 บ  protection from the master himself (remember nova? :>).  Atlantis         บ
 บ  doesn't end there however, there are many many more of the essential Op   บ
 บ  commands, Lists, and Misc options.  It even has windowing features that   บ
 บ  allow multiple logins, and shelling capabilities.                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Now for those of you that still aren't convinced.  Let's talk about   บ
 บ  the disadvantages of other scripts, namely fphoenix.  Fphoenix was nice   บ
 บ  when she (yes SHE) was updating it, but there hasn't been an update for   บ
 บ  several months.  This can lead to many annoying problems.  First of all,  บ
 บ  her "impenatrable" defenses are out of date, and I believe there are      บ
 บ  some DCC exploits that now work on it.  Another problem is all those      บ
 บ  bugs will probably never get fixed.  With Atlantis, when it first came    บ
 บ  out, Dethnite worked day and night to make sure all bugs reported were    บ
 บ  fixed.  Lack of updates aren't the only problems.  The script itself is   บ
 บ  a modification of a rip of code that's bloated in the first place.        บ
 บ  Atlantis is 100% original, making use of the newest coding techniques,    บ
 บ  which improves speed and reliablity.                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Now let me give you an idea about what happened behind the scenes.    บ
 บ  Most people don't really think about how a script came into being, so     บ
 บ  let me give you an idea.  When I first met Dethnite about 6 months ago,   บ
 บ  he had a lot of ideas he was throwing around for a new script.  While he  บ
 บ  was still writing nova, he and a few others of us sat in channel #HavoK   บ
 บ  discussing the focus of this project.  What became clear through the      บ
 บ  course of the conversation was that he wanted a script that would         บ
 บ  essentially replace fphoenix as the offering script of choice.  So, when  บ
 บ  he began coding it, he took the XDCC options into special consideration.  บ
 บ  He added a DCC status bar that allows you to see, at a glance, how much   บ
 บ  a transfer has to go.  He created the fastest, most efficient queuing     บ
 บ  system available.  Now, he's also added the first DCC RESUME ever.        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Dethnite hopes that everyone appreciates his contribution to the IRC  บ
 บ  couriering scene.  You can contact Dethnite on IRC in the channel #atl.   บ
 บ  He did not want me to give out his email, as last time it was in the      บ
 บ  script some idiots decided it'd be neat to see if he'd accually read all  บ
 บ  1000 of the mail bomb emails.  Also try not to bother him asking if he    บ
 บ  has the new version.  Just /msg atl-dcc xdcc list if it's online to get   บ
 บ  the latest update.  It should say when the newest one with resume is      บ
 บ  released.  So if the xdcc list doesn't say Atlantis with resume, it       บ
 บ  isn't the right one.                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Hitting Below the Belt                                        บ
 บ    Subject : Crystaline Death                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Hello to all those who read RCN!  This is my first article that       บ
 บ  includes two interviews in it, and it certainly won't be my last.  This   บ
 บ  interview/article talks about a release called AIDS (America is Dying     บ
 บ  Slowly) and debates on who released it, Legion or CCA?                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      There was a HUGE debate/arguement over this in channel #Legion        บ
 บ  around 11:30 am.  Personally, I didn't like it and became annoyed at the  บ
 บ  fact a group would actually steal another group's release.  So, I took    บ
 บ  the liberty to interview BOTH sides so that I remain fair.                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      The first session (below this paragraph) is with Alakazam and I.      บ
 บ  Alakazam is with CCA and will be representing CCA in this article.        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Session Start : Fri Jul 19 11:36:59 1996                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Crystalin> So, I see you are very upset?                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Alakazam> Yes.                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Crystalin> What happened?                                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Alakazam> Ok, well, Fab Five from CCA, released a program called AIDS    บ
 บ             (that stands for America Is Dying Slowly) today.  We uploaded  บ
 บ             it to tonz of sitez, over 10, put it on offerbots, etc.        บ
 บ             Anyway, Lightning and CCA couriered AIDS to a site called      บ
 บ             SynCity, which I think is Legion's HQ.  A few hours later, we  บ
 บ             checked SynCity again and we found out that someone had        บ
 บ             deleted our uploaded release and replaced it with the SAME     บ
 บ             release but under a different release group.                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Crystalin> What did you do next?                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Alakazam> Well, this really enraged my group.  We went to channel        บ
 บ             #Legion to sort this out, but they didn't have any comments.   บ
 บ             So, a colleague suggested that I inform RCN.  So here I am.    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Crystalin> So in a short sentence, summarize the main situation.         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Alakazam> Legion tried to RE-release a CCA release.  As everyone knows,  บ
 บ             CCA isn't a release group so we don't release much if          บ
 บ             anything.                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Session Close : Fri Jul 19 11:43:40 1996                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Note : This next section is an interview with Dee, a Legion senior.       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Session Start: Fri Jul 19 16:39:40 1996                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Crystalin> As we all know, you are a senior of Legion, and we at RCN     บ
 บ              would like to know how you respond to the AIDS incident with  บ
 บ              CCA?                                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Dee> What about AIDS?                                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Crystalin> Well, who released it?                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Dee> CCA released it.                                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Crystalin> Well, as Alakazam said to me earlier, you guys took their     บ
 บ              release on SynCity and you stole it.  Is that true or not?    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Dee> No, it is not.  Someone has been deleting and renaming directories  บ
 บ        to things such as CCA PUKES, etc.  Syncity is a Legion only site    บ
 บ        and I was trying to explain that to Alakazam.  However, I haven't   บ
 บ        found out who was doing the nuking.  If you logon to SynCity you    บ
 บ        will see "WTF KEEPS DELETING AND RENAMING SHIT!"                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Crystalin> So, you are basically telling me that this is a big whole     บ
 บ              misunderstanding?                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Dee> Yes.                                                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Session Close: Fri Jul 19 16:44:31 1996                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      CASE CLOSED!  Well, it finally turns out that no one has stolen       บ
 บ  anyone's release.  It just so happens that some loser out there decided   บ
 บ  to fuck around with the directories.                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I personally think that what Dee said was true.  After all, I am in   บ
 บ  Legion and I know that the people from Legion would never do such         บ
 บ  treacherous and lame acts such as stealing releases.  What's the point    บ
 บ  of stealing a release after it has been released?  There is none.  :)     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : You're Not White!                                             บ
 บ    Subject : Midnight Avian                                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      We all know that the main purpose of the whole warez scene is to      บ
 บ  bring poor individuals like us free warez!  But have you ever thought of  บ
 บ  anything else the warez scene has brought to us?  I can certainly think   บ
 บ  of a lot of them, good and bad!                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Something bad that the warez scene has brought to us is BEING         บ
 บ  UNFAIR.  For example, someone setting groups up and releases fake/old     บ
 บ  warez that no one wants just for credits on some fast boards, these       บ
 บ  people would just upload the fake/old program or game and then they       บ
 บ  would download with all the credits they have left!  That's ridiculous!   บ
 บ  If the sysop finds out that this person does cheap things like this, the  บ
 บ  sysop would lock his *alias* out, but what these people will probably do  บ
 บ  is that they will apply with a different alias and all that and do the    บ
 บ  same thing over and over again until he or she has enough credits on all  บ
 บ  the other boards to be elite!  Now is that fair to the rest of the world  บ
 บ  who really struggled at the beginning to get started while this person    บ
 บ  just gets credits for free?  NO!                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Another example, someone joins this board with an alias of someone    บ
 บ  else (on purpose) and then when that person is validated, he would send   บ
 บ  thousands and thousands of letters, both public and private messages to   บ
 บ  users with swear words.  Obviously, the sysop and all the users that      บ
 บ  read the messages will be really pissed off at this person.  (This        บ
 บ  ALIAS!) The *alias* will be logged out and it will probably be            บ
 บ  blacklisted.  If the real person with that alias tries to join the board  บ
 บ  that has that alias blacklisted (especially the board that was flooded)   บ
 บ  the sysop will immediately engage the user to CHAT and then the sysop     บ
 บ  will release all his anger on that person when it's not even his fault!   บ
 บ  Is that fair?  Of course not, but you can't blame the sysop because he    บ
 บ  doesn't know that the person who flooded the board wasn't him.            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Of course, the warez scene has also provided a tremendous amount of   บ
 บ  GOOD things to us.  The major being FREE WAREZ!!!  Everyone loves that    บ
 บ  part.  Also, it has brought all of us together as a whole with no         บ
 บ  discrimination, racism, stereotyping.  These things are found everywhere  บ
 บ  but not found in the warez scene because no one can see any other person  บ
 บ  unless they are friends and even if they see each other (maybe a meet if  บ
 บ  you live close to each other), they would have known enough about each    บ
 บ  other to not be prejudiced.                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Have you ever seen someone kicking someone out of a board/IRC         บ
 บ  channel because he/she is a member of a certain ethnic group?  Not very   บ
 บ  likely.  Have you seen someone being denied of a position in a group      บ
 บ  because he or she is fat?  Not very likely.                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      As with everything else there is always a good side and a bad side.   บ
 บ  Some people choose to stay in the warez scene, some people choose to      บ
 บ  leave the warez scene.  They all have different reasons but if you        บ
 บ  choose to leave the warez scene, hopefully it is not because my articles  บ
 บ  have bored you to death.                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  *PS* Remember, all groups are cool and should be respect if they          บ
 บ  contribute to the scene, even a little bit helps shape our scene!         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 บ    Author  : Rebel Chicken                                                 บ
 บ    Subject : Napalm Merge Fails                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Earlier this week, Prophet of Napalm proposed a merge between Napalm  บ
 บ  and Epic.  Since Epic could not seem to find the crackers to crack        บ
 บ  games, and Napalm could not seem to find the suppliers to supply games,   บ
 บ  Prophet suggested that the two games groups merge to help support their   บ
 บ  mutual needs, and thus, form a stronger games group.  Unfortunately, Bug  บ
 บ  Lord of Epic rejected Prophet's offer.  The following is a log of a       บ
 บ  conversation between Prophet and Bug Lord :                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Prophet> Are you there?                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <BugLord> Yeah?                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Prophet> I heard you guys have Close Combat.                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <BugLord> Who'd you hear it from?                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Prophet> Well, I know because the game is impossible to crack.           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <BugLord> I know.  Misha's been trying to crack it for 2 days now.        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Prophet> Are you the supplier?                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <BugLord> Nah, I didn't supply it.                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Prophet> Was Morphine the supplier?                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <BugLord> I don't know who supplied it.  I wish you hadn't spread Gender  บ
 บ            Wars though.                                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Prophet> Damn, well, I didn't.  This sucks, I want to help out Epic,     บ
 บ            but you guys don't trust me and stuff.                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <BugLord> I had that game days before Razor 1911, I just couldn't find a  บ
 บ            cracker.                                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Prophet> If you guys come to Napalm, we would help out.  I'm sure I can  บ
 บ            get Close Combat cracked.                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <BugLord> Because you're Napalm, it's kinda hard to trust other groups.   บ
 บ            There's a good chance that if Misha can't crack the game, it's  บ
 บ            safe to say it's uncrackable.                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Prophet> Yes I know, not true.  I have better crackers.  I can get it    บ
 บ            100% cracked.  I guarantee it.                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <BugLord> Misha is god at cracking.                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Prophet> That's what you guys think...                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <BugLord> Do you know anyone who's a better cracker than he is?  We       บ
 บ            already let others try to crack it, they couldn't.              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Prophet> Wayward is a better cracker.  Who else is helping to crack      บ
 บ            Close Combat?                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <BugLord> I can't say.  What do you mean by, "If you guys come to         บ
 บ            Napalm?"  You want Epic to merge with Napalm?                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Prophet> You guys can get the stuff and we can crack the stuff.          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <BugLord> Hahaha, no thanks.                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : SPA Staff                                                     บ
 บ    Subject : Standards of Piracy Association                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Formed on 6 July 1996, the SPA is an agreement between the 5 top PC   บ
 บ  games groups that lays down the official "rules of engagement" to be      บ
 บ  used in the battle to release the most.  Here is a synopsis of the        บ
 บ  topics that were discussed and voted on.  The 5 groups that met were      บ
 บ  Prestige, Razor 1911, Mantis, Napalm, and Hybrid.  Each group had         บ
 บ  approximately 2 representatives, and on the subject of voting, each       บ
 บ  group had one vote per issue.                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      1.) All 5 groups agreed that whatever was decided in the meeting      บ
 บ          would be adhered to in the releasing process.                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      2.) The 5 groups compromised on a size limit for releases.  This      บ
 บ          limit is now set at 50 1.44 meg files.  The previous limit was    บ
 บ          40 1.44 meg volumes.  In megs, this translates to approximately   บ
 บ          72 megabytes max per game.                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      3.) Groups now have the option of using 2.88 meg files instead of     บ
 บ          1.44 meg volumes should they choose to do so on a particular      บ
 บ          release.  The only catch is that ALL disks of a release must be   บ
 บ          of one format or the other.  All releases must be in either 1.44  บ
 บ          meg or 2.88 meg format.  Any games released that do not adhere    บ
 บ          to this format, or exceed the size limit (50 for 1.44's and 25    บ
 บ          for 2.88's), will be nuked for 5x credits off of all sites in     บ
 บ          the SPA.                                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      4.) The groups voted unanimously to ban all ROR releases from all     บ
 บ          sites participating in the SPA.  This means that ROR releases     บ
 บ          will be nuked for 5x credits on all sites/boards in the SPA.      บ
 บ          This ban is subject to a monthly review.                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      5.) The 5 groups decided on the name (SPA), and that meetings would   บ
 บ          be held once a month by the leaders of the 5 groups in the SPA.   บ
 บ          At these meetings issues such as volume size, group bans, and     บ
 บ          even the size limit can be discussed.                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      The SPA exists primarily to enforce fair play on the groups in the    บ
 บ  scene.  The disk limit is part of it, and banning groups like ROR that    บ
 บ  release nothing but fakes and betas (and worse package them as finals)    บ
 บ  is also a part of it.  If you run a site and would like to be SPA         บ
 บ  certified, email chemist@laker.net for more information on what you can   บ
 บ  do to help.  The SPA is interested only in fair competition for all       บ
 บ  groups big and small, and in working releases for all users regardless    บ
 บ  of what group they download.  Think of us as quality control.             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

                    ฐ฿                 ฐ฿
                     ฿                   ฿

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Killer                                                        บ
 บ    Subject : Curse or Blessing?                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      There has been much debate over small courier and releasing groups.   บ
 บ  Some say that the small groups in general hurt the scene.  Others say     บ
 บ  that the small groups actually help the scene.  After being an active     บ
 บ  participant in the BBS and internet world for the last 5 years, I think   บ
 บ  I am now in a position to present the facts in an attempt to clarify the  บ
 บ  issue.                                                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      A small group has many advantages over one of the larger ones.        บ
 บ  Smaller groups generally serve a small area (maybe just the local         บ
 บ  calling area) and less people involved.  This leads to better group       บ
 บ  control, management and organization.  The people in the group are in     บ
 บ  better contact with each other, and the local member boards.  Generally   บ
 บ  (and in all cases I have seen) this prevents the petty squabbles that     บ
 บ  plague the larger groups.  We can simply look in back issues of RCN to    บ
 บ  find examples of these juvenile power struggles.                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Smaller groups move files around local BBSes, which should be         บ
 บ  considered a blessing to the dying local scene.  Slower boards (yes       บ
 บ  there are some) find it hard to get current files and therefore find it   บ
 บ  hard to attract people who can deliver fast files.  The major courier     บ
 บ  groups sure as hell won't bother to let a smaller board join them as a    บ
 บ  member board.  The small groups help the small (slower) boards survive.   บ
 บ  After all, many people have to work their way up the ladder of the        บ
 บ  hierarchical pyramid.  Keeping the small local boards alive is a way to   บ
 บ  insure their will be people to take over when the "elite" traders         บ
 บ  retire.                                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      As hinted above smaller groups keep all people involved.  Whether it  บ
 บ  is an affiliation with the group, or simply using the files they          บ
 บ  courier.  There is always room for the scene to grow.  The only limiting  บ
 บ  factor is interest, and the number of people involved.  Small groups      บ
 บ  help create interest and keep people involved.                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      So far, all that has been discussed is small courier groups.  But     บ
 บ  there are a whole new set of problems when small releasing groups form.   บ
 บ  These small groups are notorious for releasing dupes, or non-working, or  บ
 บ  non-cracked files.  But what is the harm in this?  After a few            บ
 บ  infractions the small groups files will be banned and the group will      บ
 บ  die.  The damage done to the scene will be minor.  Since the small        บ
 บ  groups are mainly local, the damage is confined to one area code.  And    บ
 บ  small groups don't appear frequently on the Internet, the files will      บ
 บ  spread slowly (further minimizing the damage).  But occasionally, it is   บ
 บ  possible for one of these small groups to actual beat a lager group to    บ
 บ  the punch and release a program before them.  The small groups can also   บ
 บ  deal with files that the established groups might consider minor and of   บ
 บ  no concern (like 1 disk releases).  This might worry a larger group,      บ
 บ  hence the disdain the larger groups feel when looking at the smaller      บ
 บ  groups.  But for all those worried about a smaller group "moving in" on   บ
 บ  an established groups territory, you must remember the following.         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      1.) The files of smaller groups move slower, they are not usually on  บ
 บ          the Internet.                                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      2.) Most people would go for a DOD util over a no-name group util.    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      3.) Even if a small group releases a file faster than a large group,  บ
 บ          only a few small waves will be created in the hypothetical        บ
 บ          trading pool.                                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Small groups can do much good (especially for a dying area code) and  บ
 บ  do relatively little damage.  So why do people look down on them?  It     บ
 บ  might be an unjustified fear of a "new up and comer," or it might be an   บ
 บ  ego boost.  The small groups should not be frowned upon, but encouraged.  บ
 บ  After all even Microsoft started small.                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 บ    Author  : Rebel Chicken                                                 บ
 บ    Subject : Group Reviews : Games                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Hello, and welcome to Reality Check Network's all new group review!   บ
 บ  Here I will be reviewing the 5 best games release groups in the scene.    บ
 บ  Well, actually, *I* won't be the one reviewing them, *THEY* will be!      บ
 บ  It's all up to the groups, this is where quantity DOES count, but you     บ
 บ  will soon enough find that quality by far outweighs quantity.  Let's      บ
 บ  review the criteria I'll be using for judging releases.  The following    บ
 บ  is the scoring basis I'll be using :                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Points :                                                                  บ
 บ  --------                                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [-3] The game didn't work and a crack/fix was not released within 72      บ
 บ       hours.  The group may regain the 3 lost points by releasing a crack  บ
 บ       or fix, even beyond the 3 day period.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 1] The game was a dupe or freeware,                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 2] Unsatisfactory,                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 3] Average,                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 4] Above Average, and                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 5] Excellent!                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      A group may lose points the following week and have their releases    บ
 บ  labeled as broken (thus receiving the proper amout of points).  If the    บ
 บ  group has released a fix between the two issues, we'll give them credit   บ
 บ  accordingly.  If a group releases a fix within a 3 day period, the        บ
 บ  game will be rated as if it worked in the first place, thus getting the   บ
 บ  3 points it lost back and any points it would have earned.  If a group    บ
 บ  releases a fix after the 3 day period has expired, it will receive its 3  บ
 บ  points back, but get no more.  Betas may receive no more than 3 points.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ฬออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออน
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ                                                                            บ

 บ  [-3] The game didn't work and a crack/fix was not released within 72      บ

 บ  [ 1] The game was a dupe or freeware,                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 2] Unsatisfactory,                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 3] Average,                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 4] Above Average, and                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 5] Excellent!                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      A group may lose points the following week and have their releases    บ
 บ  labeled as broken (thus receiving the proper amout of points).  If the    บ
 บ  group has released a fix between the two issues, we'll give them credit   บ

 บ                                                                            บ

                                         ฿     r e v i e w s !

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Rebel Chicken                                                 บ
 บ    Subject : Group Reviews : Games                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Hello, and welcome to Reality Check Network's all new group review!   บ
 บ  Here I will be reviewing the 5 best games release groups in the scene.    บ
 บ  Well, actually, *I* won't be the one reviewing them, *THEY* will be!      บ
 บ  It's all up to the groups, this is where quantity DOES count, but you     บ
 บ  will soon enough find that quality by far outweighs quantity.  Let's      บ
 บ  review the criteria I'll be using for judging releases.  The following    บ
 บ  is the scoring basis I'll be using :                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Points :                                                                  บ
 บ  --------                                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [-3] The game didn't work and a crack/fix was not released within 72      บ
 บ       hours.  The group may regain the 3 lost points by releasing a crack  บ
 บ       or fix, even beyond the 3 day period.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 1] The game was a dupe or freeware,                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 2] Unsatisfactory,                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 3] Average,                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 4] Above Average, and                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 5] Excellent!                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      A group may lose points the following week and have their releases    บ
 บ  labeled as broken (thus receiving the proper amout of points).  If the    บ
 บ  group has released a fix between the two issues, we'll give them credit   บ
 บ  accordingly.  If a group releases a fix within a 3 day period, the        บ
 บ  game will be rated as if it worked in the first place, thus getting the   บ
 บ  3 points it lost back and any points it would have earned.  If a group    บ
 บ  releases a fix after the 3 day period has expired, it will receive its 3  บ
 บ  points back, but get no more.  Betas may receive no more than 3 points.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ฬออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออน
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  ฺฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฟ  บ
 บ  ณ            Dates of Games Reviewed : 07/04/96 -> 07/10/96            ณ  บ
 บ  ภฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤู  บ

                                         ฿     r e v i e w s !

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Rebel Chicken                                                 บ
 บ    Subject : Group Reviews : Games                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Hello, and welcome to Reality Check Network's all new group review!   บ
 บ  Here I will be reviewing the 5 best games release groups in the scene.    บ
 บ  Well, actually, *I* won't be the one reviewing them, *THEY* will be!      บ
 บ  It's all up to the groups, this is where quantity DOES count, but you     บ
 บ  will soon enough find that quality by far outweighs quantity.  Let's      บ
 บ  review the criteria I'll be using for judging releases.  The following    บ
 บ  is the scoring basis I'll be using :                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Points :                                                                  บ
 บ  --------                                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [-3] The game didn't work and a crack/fix was not released within 72      บ
 บ       hours.  The group may regain the 3 lost points by releasing a crack  บ
 บ       or fix, even beyond the 3 day period.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 1] The game was a dupe or freeware,                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 2] Unsatisfactory,                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 3] Average,                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 4] Above Average, and                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 5] Excellent!                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      A group may lose points the following week and have their releases    บ
 บ  labeled as broken (thus receiving the proper amout of points).  If the    บ
 บ  group has released a fix between the two issues, we'll give them credit   บ
 บ  accordingly.  If a group releases a fix within a 3 day period, the        บ
 บ  game will be rated as if it worked in the first place, thus getting the   บ
 บ  3 points it lost back and any points it would have earned.  If a group    บ
 บ  releases a fix after the 3 day period has expired, it will receive its 3  บ
 บ  points back, but get no more.  Betas may receive no more than 3 points.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ฬออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออน
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  ฺฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฟ  บ
 บ  ณ            Dates of Games Reviewed : 07/11/96 -> 07/17/96            ณ  บ
 บ  ภฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤู  บ

 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Rebel Chicken                                                 บ
 บ    Subject : Group Reviews : Utils                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Hello, and welcome to Reality Check Network's all new group review!   บ
 บ  Here I will be reviewing the 5 best utils release groups in the scene.    บ
 บ  Well, actually, *I* won't be the one reviewing them, *THEY* will be!      บ
 บ  It's all up to the groups, this is where quantity DOES count, but you     บ
 บ  will soon enough find that quality by far outweighs quantity.  Let's      บ
 บ  review the criteria I'll be using for judging releases.  The following    บ
 บ  is the scoring basis I'll be using :                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Points :                                                                  บ
 บ  --------                                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [-3] The util didn't work and a crack/fix was not released within 72      บ
 บ       hours.  The group may regain the 3 lost points by releasing a crack  บ
 บ       or fix, even beyond the 3 day period.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 1] The util was a dupe or freeware,                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 2] Unsatisfactory,                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 3] Average,                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 4] Above Average, and                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 5] Excellent!                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      A group may lose points the following week and have their releases    บ
 บ  labeled as broken (thus receiving the proper amout of points).  If the    บ
 บ  group has released a fix between the two issues, we'll give them credit   บ
 บ  accordingly.  If a group releases a fix within a 3 day period, the        บ
 บ  util will be rated as if it worked in the first place, thus getting the   บ
 บ  3 points it lost back and any points it would have earned.  If a group    บ
 บ  releases a fix after the 3 day period has expired, it will receive its 3  บ
 บ  points back, but get no more.  Betas may receive no more than 3 points.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ฬออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออน
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  ฺฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฟ  บ
 บ  ณ            Dates of Utils Reviewed : 06/20/96 -> 06/26/96            ณ  บ

 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Rebel Chicken                                                 บ
 บ    Subject : Group Reviews : Utils                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Hello, and welcome to Reality Check Network's all new group review!   บ
 บ  Here I will be reviewing the 5 best utils release groups in the scene.    บ
 บ  Well, actually, *I* won't be the one reviewing them, *THEY* will be!      บ
 บ  It's all up to the groups, this is where quantity DOES count, but you     บ
 บ  will soon enough find that quality by far outweighs quantity.  Let's      บ
 บ  review the criteria I'll be using for judging releases.  The following    บ
 บ  is the scoring basis I'll be using :                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Points :                                                                  บ
 บ  --------                                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [-3] The util didn't work and a crack/fix was not released within 72      บ
 บ       hours.  The group may regain the 3 lost points by releasing a crack  บ
 บ       or fix, even beyond the 3 day period.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 1] The util was a dupe or freeware,                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 2] Unsatisfactory,                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 3] Average,                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 4] Above Average, and                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 5] Excellent!                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      A group may lose points the following week and have their releases    บ
 บ  labeled as broken (thus receiving the proper amout of points).  If the    บ
 บ  group has released a fix between the two issues, we'll give them credit   บ
 บ  accordingly.  If a group releases a fix within a 3 day period, the        บ
 บ  util will be rated as if it worked in the first place, thus getting the   บ
 บ  3 points it lost back and any points it would have earned.  If a group    บ
 บ  releases a fix after the 3 day period has expired, it will receive its 3  บ
 บ  points back, but get no more.  Betas may receive no more than 3 points.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ฬออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออน
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  ฺฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฟ  บ
 บ  ณ            Dates of Utils Reviewed : 06/26/96 -> 07/03/96            ณ  บ
 บ  ภฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤู  บ
