 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Rebel Chicken                                                 บ
 บ    Subject : Group Reviews : Utils                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Hello, and welcome to Reality Check Network's all new group review!   บ
 บ  Here I will be reviewing the 5 best utils release groups in the scene.    บ
 บ  Well, actually, *I* won't be the one reviewing them, *THEY* will be!      บ
 บ  It's all up to the groups, this is where quantity DOES count, but you     บ
 บ  will soon enough find that quality by far outweighs quantity.  Let's      บ
 บ  review the criteria I'll be using for judging releases.  The following    บ
 บ  is the scoring basis I'll be using :                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Points :                                                                  บ
 บ  --------                                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [-3] The util didn't work and a crack/fix was not released within 72      บ
 บ       hours.  The group may regain the 3 lost points by releasing a crack  บ
 บ       or fix, even beyond the 3 day period.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 1] The util was a dupe or freeware,                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 2] Unsatisfactory,                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 3] Average,                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 4] Above Average, and                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 5] Excellent!                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      A group may lose points the following week and have their releases    บ
 บ  labeled as broken (thus receiving the proper amout of points).  If the    บ
 บ  group has released a fix between the two issues, we'll give them credit   บ
 บ  accordingly.  If a group releases a fix within a 3 day period, the        บ
 บ  util will be rated as if it worked in the first place, thus getting the   บ
 บ  3 points it lost back and any points it would have earned.  If a group    บ
 บ  releases a fix after the 3 day period has expired, it will receive its 3  บ
 บ  points back, but get no more.  Betas may receive no more than 3 points.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ฬออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออน
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  ฺฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฟ  บ
 บ  ณ            Dates of Utils Reviewed : 07/04/96 -> 07/10/96            ณ  บ
 บ  ภฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤู  บ

 บ    Author  : Rebel Chicken                                                 บ
 บ    Subject : Group Reviews : Utils                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Hello, and welcome to Reality Check Network's all new group review!   บ
 บ  Here I will be reviewing the 5 best utils release groups in the scene.    บ
 บ  Well, actually, *I* won't be the one reviewing them, *THEY* will be!      บ
 บ  It's all up to the groups, this is where quantity DOES count, but you     บ
 บ  will soon enough find that quality by far outweighs quantity.  Let's      บ
 บ  review the criteria I'll be using for judging releases.  The following    บ
 บ  is the scoring basis I'll be using :                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Points :                                                                  บ
 บ  --------                                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [-3] The util didn't work and a crack/fix was not released within 72      บ
 บ       hours.  The group may regain the 3 lost points by releasing a crack  บ
 บ       or fix, even beyond the 3 day period.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 1] The util was a dupe or freeware,                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 2] Unsatisfactory,                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 3] Average,                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 4] Above Average, and                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 5] Excellent!                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      A group may lose points the following week and have their releases    บ
 บ  labeled as broken (thus receiving the proper amout of points).  If the    บ
 บ  group has released a fix between the two issues, we'll give them credit   บ
 บ  accordingly.  If a group releases a fix within a 3 day period, the        บ
 บ  util will be rated as if it worked in the first place, thus getting the   บ
 บ  3 points it lost back and any points it would have earned.  If a group    บ
 บ  releases a fix after the 3 day period has expired, it will receive its 3  บ
 บ  points back, but get no more.  Betas may receive no more than 3 points.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Trip                                                          บ
 บ    Subject : Carding                                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Before you even think about carding something, you should know that   บ
 บ  you can get in BIG trouble if you get caught.  Carding is a federal       บ
 บ  offense, so just be careful and smart.  Here is what you will need to     บ
 บ  card something :                                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      1.) A Credit Card.                                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      2.) A drop off site.                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      3.) An online store that delivers gift orders (a different address    บ
 บ          than the cardholder's address).                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      First off, you will need a credit card with FULL information.  This   บ
 บ  must include the cardholder's FULL name, address, credit card number      บ
 บ  with experation date, phone number, city, state, zip code, bank name,     บ
 บ  and card type.  Next, you will need to find a house somewhere in your     บ
 บ  neighborhood which is vacant.  Don't even think of carding something to   บ
 บ  a house with a big "For Sale" sign in front of it, cause they won't       บ
 บ  deliver it there.  If you know somebody who is on vacation, you could     บ
 บ  use their house.                                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Now you need to find an online store.  You can card by phone, but it  บ
 บ  is much easier just doing it all online.  To find online stores, I        บ
 บ  recommend getting a computer magazine (if you wanna get some computer     บ
 บ  stuff) such as "Computer Shopper."  This magazine is about 800 pages and  บ
 บ  is ALL advertisements for computer stores.  Now go to the online store,   บ
 บ  and find the product you want.  Have it sent either "second day air," or  บ
 บ  "express delivery."  Next day delivery is usually too suspicious, and     บ
 บ  the store will call the credit card holder back to verify the order.      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      A few days later, you should be ready to go pick up the package.      บ
 บ  Only go to pick it up late at night, like sometime after 10:00 pm would   บ
 บ  be good.  Make sure that there is nobody around when you go to pick it    บ
 บ  up because you don't want to end up in jail.  If the package is not       บ
 บ  there, then wait a couple more days, and if it isn't there within a       บ
 บ  week, try carding it again.  It took me 2 times to card my RAM a few      บ
 บ  months ago, and I had it send second day express and it didn't get        บ
 บ  delivered for 7 days.  :(                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Tips :                                                                    บ
 บ  ------                                                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      1.) You might want to write a note and leave it on the door of your   บ
 บ          drop off site before the package gets delivered.  Have the note   บ
 บ          say that you work from 9 to 5 every day and ask that they please  บ
 บ          leave package on the doorstep.  Then, sign it with the signature  บ
 บ          of the person you had it sent to, NOT your name.                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      2.) Don't use the same drop site more than once.                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      3.) If the online store asks you for an email address, just use one   บ
 บ          that you know is valid but NOT your own.                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  *PS* Have phun and don't get caught.                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ      Welcome to Dear Road Rebel!  This is going to be YOUR column that is  บ
 บ  a cross between Dear Abby and Dave Berry.  The most important part of     บ
 บ  this is YOUR participation.  If you have ever had a question about the    บ
 บ  scene or just a comment, here's the place!  Have you ever wanted to know  บ
 บ  why some people do this or that?  ASK!  I would love to take it to the    บ
 บ  extreme for you and we will be happy to research it!  I hope you have as  บ
 บ  much fun with this as I will!  Remember, this is YOUR column!             บ

 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Dear Road Rebel,                                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Carding has never meant that much to me.  I've never really gotten    บ
 บ  into it, and the only reason I ever did it was to see if it would work    บ
 บ  (which it did).  But, frankly put, it's stupid.  People don't seem to     บ
 บ  understand the risk involved.  For example, how many people in the last   บ
 บ  few years have gotten caught specifically for warez                       บ
 บ  releasing/couriering?  I don't have an exact statistic, but I wouldn't    บ
 บ  say very many.  Most people who get busted are busted for another         บ
 บ  reason, such as hacking, kiddie porn (as in the case of Anarchist), and   บ
 บ  carding.  It's just another thing that gets you in more trouble.  When    บ
 บ  people get busted for carding computer stuff, they get there computer     บ
 บ  searched.  And when they find warez they get busted for that too.  It's   บ
 บ  not a good idea, and not as safe as people think.  I'm not going to go    บ
 บ  on some big crusade to stop people from doing it.  Just be careful.       บ
 บ  Thanks for your time.                                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                               Signed,                      บ
 บ                                                  Double O Zero             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Dear Double O Zero,  Well, a lot of people think you can just do it and   บ
 บ  never get caught.  Carding is one of the most watched out for things you  บ
 บ  can do anymore.  But yeah, if you are busted for something stupid like    บ
 บ  kiddy porn (Entropy) the cops would sure as heel like to tag you with a   บ
 บ  credit fraud charge also.  BUT a lot of people still get away with it,    บ
 บ  and I hope they keep getting away with it.  Screw the credit companies!   บ
 บ                                               Signed,                      บ
 บ                                                  Road Rebel                บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป

 บ    Author  : Rebel Chicken                                                 บ
 บ    Subject : Before ROR and Reflux...                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I was minding my own business one day while browsing through some     บ
 บ  oldwarez sites when I stumbled upon a "Mortal.Kombat.3" directory.  I     บ
 บ  have been looking for this game for a while now and I was quite happy     บ
 บ  that this site still had it.  I happily leeched all the tdumk3*.zip       บ
 บ  files.  After installing MK3, and just plain screwing around, I found     บ
 บ  myself very disappointed with the fact that I could not do any of the     บ
 บ  fatalities or special moves.  I remembered that there was a mk3codes.txt  บ
 บ  on that site which I had passed by.  I decided to pay that site another   บ
 บ  visit.                                                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Upon reading mk3codes.txt, I was surprised to see that this text      บ
 บ  file was written by Tklp.  At that time, Tklp was a senior of this lame   บ
 บ  group called uh... LAME.  Not only did I learn my favorite MK3            บ
 บ  fatalities and special moves, I also learned that before Tklp was busy    บ
 บ  releasing beta games that were hex edited to say they were the final,     บ
 บ  Tklp was busy writing cheat codes and special moves and then releasing    บ
 บ  them as text files.  At least he made himself useful back then, perhaps   บ
 บ  he should have stuck with it.                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Now, what really makes me laugh is that this mk3codes.txt also has a  บ
 บ  phone number at the bottom of it.  Tklp says that if anyone has problem   บ
 บ  with the MK3 cheat codes, they should call him at this number.  I don't   บ
 บ  know if the phone number still works, I never bothered to test it.        บ
 บ  Remember, I found this text file on an oldwarez site, the following       บ
 บ  document could have been leeched by ANYONE...                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ

 บ                           MORTAL KOMBAT 3                                  บ
 บ                     (FINISHING MOVES AND CODES)                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                            KOMBAT KODES                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  ENTER CODE SYMBOLS AT MATCH-UP SCREEN WITH THE LOW PUNCH, BLOCK AND LOW   บ
 บ  BUTTONS ON BOTH SIDES OF THE MACHINES. THE NUMBERS SHOW HOW MANY TIMES E  บ
 บ  BUTTON SHOULD BE PRESSED, FROM ZERO TO NINE; ADVANCE THROUGH THE LIST IN  บ
 บ  REVERSE BY HOLDING THE JOYSTICK UP(i.e. INSTEAD OF PRESSING A BUTTON NIN  บ
 บ  TIMES TO GET THE SKULL SYMBOL, JUST HOLD UP AND HIT THE BUTTON ONCE.)     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  THROWING DISABLED: 100-100                                                บ
 บ  BLOCKING DISABLED: 020-020                                                บ
 บ  1/2 ENERGY PLAYER 1: 033-000                                              บ
 บ  1/2 ENERGY PLAYER 2: 000-033                                              บ
 บ  1/4 ENERGY PLAYER 1: 707-000                                              บ
 บ  1/4 ENERGY PLAYER 2: 000-707                                              บ
 บ  INFINITE RUN: 466-466                                                     บ
 บ  REMOVE ENERGY BARS: 987-123                                               บ
 บ  DARK KOMBAT: 688-422                                                      บ
 บ  RANDOM MORPH: 460-460                                                     บ
 บ  PSYCHO KOMBAT: 985-125                                                    บ
 บ  NO FEAR: 282-282                                                          บ
 บ  THEATER OF MAGIC: 987-666                                                 บ
 บ  KNOWLEDGE IS POWER: 123-926                                               บ
 บ  HIDDEN SHOOTER GAME: 642-468                                              บ
 บ  FIGHT SMOKE: 205-205                                                      บ
 บ  FIGHT MOTARO: 969-141                                                     บ
 บ  FIGHT SHAO KAHN: 033-564                                                  บ
 บ  FIGHT NOOB SAIBOT: 769-141                                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  and ..........                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  THE ULTIMATE KOMBAT KODE: 10902-22234                                     บ
 บ  Once entered you can play as Smoke and will never need to be entered      บ
 บ  again.                                                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  THE RULES TO DOING BABALITIES,FRIENDSHIPS,ETC. and HOW TO PERFORM THEM!   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  BABALITIES/FRIENDSHIPS:                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  TO DO A BABAL. OR FRIEND. YOU CANNOT BLOCK DURING THE ROUND IN WHICH      บ
 บ  YOU ARE GOING TO DO THE BABAL. OR FRIEND.                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  HAVE MERCY(FEEL SORRY FOR THEM AND GIVE THEM MORE ENERGY)!                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  DURING THE THIRD ROUND WHEN IT SAYS "FINISH HIM",STAND FAR AWAY           บ
 บ  AND HOLD RUN, PRESS DOWN FOUR TIMES, THEN RELEASE RUN!YOUR ENEMY          บ
 บ  GETS A LITTLE MORE ENERGY! YOU MUST SHOW MERCY IN ORDER TO PERFORM        บ
 บ  AN ANIMALITY!                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  ANIMALITIES:                                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  THE NEW MOVES THAT WERE ONCE ONLY A RUMOR IN MORTAL KOMBAT 1 AND 2        บ
 บ  ARE NOW TRUE! IN ORDER TO PERFORM THEM YOU MUST SHOW MERCY(TO SHOW        บ
 บ  MERCY READ HAVE MERCY, IT IS ABOVE THIS ARTICLE)!                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ  YOUR OPPONENT!                                                            บ

 บ  This is some lame ass game but its a game! The name tends to make you     บ

 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Prophet is right.  This Napalm release REALLY is a lame ass game.     บ
 บ  You see, this game comes with the ID4 action figures.  I guess Napalm is  บ
 บ  REAL quality.  What I don't understand is, if Prophet even admits that    บ
 บ  this game sucks, then why the hell release it?  Oh, I know why...         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      "This is some lame ass game but its a game!"                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      What Prophet meant to say is, "This is some lame ass game, but it's   บ
 บ  a release!  I don't care about quality, I'll release anything!"           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      "The name tends to make you think its some really lame game but its   บ
 บ  actually ID4: The Game!"                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      What Prophet meant to say is, "The game is lame.  The name of the     บ
 บ  game tends to make you think its lame, but the game is actually not       บ
 บ  lame."                                                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  *PS* The ID4 movie was great, I loved it, but the game that comes with    บ
 บ       the action figures really sucked.                                    บ

 บ  ณ                                                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  From the makers of other card games comes Pinochle for Windows/Win '95    บ
 บ  (which is by far their best effort yet).  Featuring pretty graphics,      บ
 บ  this ereet game even has network play, allowing you to play fast-paced    บ
 บ  games of skill over the modem/LAN with buddies.  To hell with Duke Nuke   บ
 บ  'Em, now you can have what you REALLY want - Pinochlematches to the       บ
 บ  death!                                                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      The Renegade Chemist calls himself the The Budget Chemist here        บ
 บ  because he knows that this shit release sells for $9.99... how do I       บ
 บ  know?  I work at Egghead.  I'm writing this so The Budget Chemist here    บ
 บ  will never again be stupid enough to go out of his way and put down       บ
 บ  other games group for releasing budget...                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  To install, unpack PINOCHLE.ARJ into a dir.  Then run SETUP.EXE.  Once    บ
 บ  you've installed it, make a dir in the directory installed to called      บ
 บ  BPIN (ex. C:\PINOCHLE\BPIN).  Now go into the dir you installed FROM and  บ
 บ  copy the files from the \BICYCLE\BPIN subdir into the dir you just made.  บ
 บ  Let me give you an example. Let's say we installed from C:\TEST to        บ
 บ  C:\PINOCHLE First go into C:\PINOCHLE and make a sub dir called BPIN, so  บ
 บ  you have C:\PINOCHLE\BPIN.  Copy everything from C:\TEST\BICYCLE\BPIN     บ
 บ  into C:\PINOCHLE\BPIN.  Once all that is done, run CRACK.COM in the       บ
 บ  C:\PINOCHLE directory.  Sorry about the jury rigging, but this was a      บ
 บ  pain to reroute.                                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Fucking Ay!  Do I need to be a rocket scientist to figure out how to  บ
 บ  install a fucking lame ass budget card game?  Can't you guys just make    บ
 บ  an INSTALL.EXE to do it FOR ME?  Maybe I should ask Xenon to help you     บ
 บ  guys...                                                                   บ

  ฑ to courier files.. you must have references and/or your own         ฑ
  ฑ resources (as in trade sites) where you get your own supply of      ฑ
  ฑ warez. As always, we are looking for talented programmers, phreaks, ฑ
  ฑ shell suppliers and of course, FTP site operators.                  ฑ

ณ        ~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~                                               ณ
ณ Request to Send is a high-speed high-volume couriering group whose          ณ
ณ     purpose is to unite the top echelon of elite traders in an environment  ณ
ณ     which facilitates a constant flow of quality warez & a damn good time.  ณ
ณ     No dictators, no egoshit, no assholes.                                  ณ
ณ                                                                             ณ
ณ       -Slots are always open for dedicated and resourceful couriers-        ณ
ณ           -Large boards and sites are encouraged to contact us-             ณ
ณ            -Follow our flaming debris down the superhighway-                ณ
ณ          -or leave a detailed message to an147791@anon.penet.fi-            ณ
ณ                                                                             ณ
ณ RTS continues to uphold its policy against pre/double-tagging and stripping ณ
ณ You are ensured that all files bearing the RTS logo went through us -FIRST- ณ
ณ                                                                             ณ
ณ                                                                             ณ
ณO  Welcome to long days, warm weather and sunny skies.                      .ณ

                         ๚๙๚ G R E E T S  ๙  N E W S ๚๙๚
 ฺฤฟฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฟฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤ
 ภฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤ๙๚๚ ๚ ๚๚๙ฤฤมฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤ ฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤ ฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤ ฤฤฤฤฤ๙๙๙ ๙๙ ๙
 ณ ณ                   ณ Acidplain has been kicked out of Legion by a
 ณ ณ                   ณ unanimous vote by the group.  He decided to say that
 ณ ณ                   ณ he quit the group to make himself look better.
 ณ ณ   ๚๙๚ NEWS ๚๙๚    ณ
 ณ ณ                   ณ And he also claimed he would bring members that
 ณ ณ                   ณ went with him into PWA when he left. But the next
 ณ ณ                   ณ day, when we did a /whois on him, it says:
 ณ ณ                   ณ Acidplain Rzr/Malice/Pnc. For what we know, PNC
 ณ ณ                   ณ said Acidplain was never in PNC. And as for Malice,
 ณ ณ                   ณ one of the council is kicking him out since he's no
 ณ ณ                   ณ longer in Legion. Last but not least, he's not in
 ณ ณ                   ณ Razor. We thought we'd just like to clear this up
 ณ ณ                   ณ for you people.
 ณ ณ                   ณ
 ณ ณ                   ณ Violence, a small utils group, has merged into
 ณ ณ                   ณ Legion.  It looks like a peaceful merge so far...
 ณ ณ                   ณ
 ณ ณ                   ณ We'd like to welcome Syncity as our new HQ site,
 ณ ณ                   ณ and Zion with his BBS HQ, Zion's Hideout.
 ฺฤฟฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฟฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤ
 ภฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤ๙๚๚ ๚ ๚๚๙ฤฤมฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤ ฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤ ฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤ ฤฤฤฤฤ๙๙๙ ๙๙ ๙
 ณ ณ                   ณ If you are applying as a courier, don't bother.  We
 ณ ณ                   ณ are currently in need of suppliers, crackers, card
 ณ ณ ๚๙๚ COMMENTS ๚๙๚  ณ suppliers, and siteops.  If you can do any of the
 ณ ณ                   ณ above and would like to join, come onto the Efnet,
 ณ ณ                   ณ join #LEGiON, and talk a council member.
 ฺฤฟฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฟฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤ

 ณ     variety of games, and hopefully all groups will continue to release    ณ
 ณ     quality cracks under the new 50 DISKETTE MAXIMUM.                      ณ

 ณ Group News:                                                             ณ
 ณ                                                                         ณ
 ณ              Make sure to check our www, Adress below.                  ณ
 ณ              Rebels are now also looking for a GOOD vga artist,         ณ
 ณ              that can help us design and improve our www side           ณ
 ณ              If you think that you can help us contact us in any        ณ
 ณ              way mentioned in this .nfo.                                ณ
 ณ                                                                         ณ
 ณ                                                                         ณ
 ณ              We are trying to be a group with a 100 % brisk and loyal   ณ
 ณ              members. We are doing it in our way and for fun...         ณ
 ณ              We all have a life outside the scene and this is a great   ณ
 ณ              hobby activity. Thats a fact! We can always take a few     ณ
 ณ              days/weeks off from the scene, but we will always be back  ณ
 ณ              strong as usual, so friends who used to be a part of our   ณ
 ณ              great team, time to wake up!                               ณ
 ณ              And please...contact us if you wanna be a proud            ณ
 ณ              REBELS member again.                                       ณ
 ณ                                                                         ณ
 ณ              We are a living legend with a history back to the c64 days.ณ
 ณ              We ruled the Amiga demoscene in many ways and now we are   ณ
 ณ              a major part of the PC scene. We can die but never cease   ณ
 ณ              to exist for all who know what we have done.               ณ
 ณ                                                                         ณ
 ณ              If you wanna reach us for joining or for another reason    ณ
 ณ              please contact any member on IRC or send a mail on e-mail  ณ
 ณ              met.asa@mbox200.swipnet.se                                 ณ
 ณ                                                                         ณ
 ณ              Do NOT forget that contacts only can be accepted with      ณ
 ณ              a good attitude and respect for our name!                  ณ

 ณ                                                                         ณ

 ณ  Warm welcome to Drag and Toxic! as a senior member!                       ณ
 ณ                                                                            ณ
 ณ  If you are going to apply to us, please read lines bellow:                ณ
 ณ                                                                            ณ
 ณ  - We do not need net couriers, artists, ppecoders.                        ณ
 ณ  - If you are a supplier and wanna join us then you have to be  able  to   ณ
 ณ    supply one or two releases per week at least. And offer  something we   ณ
 ณ    can release when you apply to. And please don't forget everything you   ณ
 ณ    supply must be the quality ware, not just worthless stuff  like  docs   ณ
 ณ    or shareware and freeware utils or games.                               ณ
 ณ  - If you are a cracker, you must be able to do donggle and crack  warez   ณ
 ณ    that use DOS4GW.                                                        ณ
 ณ  - If you are a sysop, you have to run 5+ node board  and  do  not  even   ณ
 ณ    think to just run board, all Sodom sysops are actively  participating   ณ
 ณ    in the success of the group.                                            ณ
 ณ  - If you are a siteop, you have to run 50-100 kb/sec site and  have  6+   ณ
 ณ    gigz disk size at least.                                                ณ
 ณ  - If you are a LD caller, you have to be able to move 10+ megz a day and  ณ
 ณ    supply calling cards.                                                   ณ
 ณ                                                                            ณ
 ณ  If you can't offer us everything we want then don't bother us applying!   ณ

 บ   This is the 23rd issue of Reality Check Network.  Our goal is to bring   บ
 บ   the most interesting news to the public in a way revolutionizing the     บ
 บ   scene each and every week!!!  Look to us for the latest in scene news,   บ
 บ   articles, interviews, and loads of fun, every other Sunday!!!            บ

 บ                  see them threatened.  We will not die for them until      บ
 บ                  they are taken away.  With considerable horror, we watch  บ
 บ                  men of other nations allow themselves to be robbed of     บ
 บ                  their right to their opinions.  But, more insidiously,    บ
 บ                  we now accept dictated predications which we are told to  บ
 บ                  use in coming to conclusions.  Those who know the         บ
 บ                  LEAST... obey the BEST. - Anonymous                       บ

 บ      RCN is proud to present to the scene the official RCN t-shirt.  We    บ
 บ  tried to keep the price as low as we could so that everyone can enjoy     บ
 บ  these goodies.  Keeping with RCN's volunteerish spirit to help the scene, บ
 บ  Road Rebel has decided to take it upon himself to make the RCN t-shirts   บ
 บ  available to the masses.  This is a non-profit venture and we hope that   บ
 บ  in many ways, RCN continues to benefit the scene.. even when we are not   บ
 บ  near our computers.                                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ       The RCN logo is approximately 8"x6" printed on the back of a        บ
 บ        HEAVY-duty Fruit of the Loom white t-shirt, the front is plain.     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ       A preview of the shirt can viewed upon pressing escape.             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ       Special orders take up to 4 weeks for shipping.                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ  Summary :                                                                 บ
 บ  ---------                                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  1.) All RCN issues must be online and available for FREE download.  The   บ
 บ      current issue and back issues must be located in separate file        บ
 บ      directories.  The FULL file_id.diz for the current issue must be      บ
 บ      shown.                                                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  2.) A "Reality Check Network" conference must be set up.  The "rcn        บ
 บ      affiliate board" ansi must be shown somewhere in the login process    บ
 บ      or somewhere in the conference join.                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  3.) Sysops must notify all bulletin board users, via nonconference        บ
 บ      specific mass email, of the new issues available for free download.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      The new update to the Reality Check Network World Wide Web Site,      บ
 บ  http://www.rcn.org/, adds many new features :                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ       Speed Optimization : RCN.org is now speed optimized, which means    บ
 บ        you spend less time waiting and more time browsing.                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ       Better Back Issue Access : It's now quick and easy to scan through  บ
 บ        RCN's back issues, each one has its full description online, to     บ
 บ        make searching for the desired issue that much easier.              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ       Better Interface : v2.0 brings an end to the confusing              บ
 บ        conglomeration of pages that previously had existed.  Now speed     บ
 บ        through the icon driven interface to scan back issues of RCN and    บ
 บ        other emags, send comments, read credits, and check out             บ
 บ        merchandise and free files.                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ       Text or JAVA Version : Whatever browser you use can now access the  บ
 บ        RCN.org pages.  Before only Netscape was allowed, but now LYNX and  บ
 บ        other text base users can now access the pages.                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ       New Look Graphics : The new graphics style are a nice change of     บ
 บ        pace from the hard-edged style of before.                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      To become a file mirror, contact us in #RCN on IRC, you must be able  บ
 บ  to store all back issues in a publically accessible directory from the    บ
 บ  WWW.  A link will be created from RCN.org to your site, so users can      บ
 บ  acquire issues from there if the main site becomes overloaded.            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      RCN WWW Site       : http://www.rcn.org/                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      RCN Mirror Site #1 : http://www.halcyon.com/sbecker                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
